Li Guojie Sentenced to Three Years in Prison

Chen Fumu's Trial Suspended Pending Arrest

Bribe of 700,000 Taels of Silver to Foreigners to be Recovered and Confiscated

Li Guojie, the general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Chen Fumu, the concurrent supervisor, were accused of privately borrowing foreign debts and signing loan contracts with the American-owned China Trading Corporation using the wharves and docks, as well as leasing merchant ships from the Dalae Steamship Company, which harmed navigation rights, and of delivering a bribe of 700,000 taels of silver to Chen Fumu. The local court pronounced its verdict yesterday afternoon at 2 PM. After lunch, the first courtroom was already filled with people who had come to listen. Therefore, the court dispatched police chiefs Chen Junfang and police officers Chen Xihui and Zhu Wenqing to maintain order. Li Guojie was brought from the Shanghai Hospital. Soon after, the criminal court judge Qian Chengjun, judges Shen Youqi and Sun Xiaolou, prosecutor Xie Lian, and clerk Jiang Meixuan all arrived at the court. Li Guojie and his defense lawyers Jiang Yiping and Sha Xunyi arrived at court. The presiding judge Qian Chengjun stood up and read the verdict: "Li Guojie, together with others, violated his duties, causing damage to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and is sentenced to two years of imprisonment and deprived of his civil rights for four years. He also violated his duties by delivering a bribe, and is sentenced to two years of imprisonment and deprived of his civil rights for four years. The sentences will be served concurrently for a total of three years of imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for four years. The number of days of detention prior to the final judgment will be deducted from the prison sentence at a rate of two days for each day. Chen Fumu's trial is suspended. The bribe of 700,000 taels of silver will be recovered and confiscated." After the verdict was pronounced, the reasons for the judgment were read to Li Guojie. The reasons were roughly as follows: if the treaty was not fulfilled as stipulated in the contract, there was the right to confiscate it and dispose of it according to American law, and the items such as borrowing money from Dalae to buy ships and inserting American flags were all matters of losing rights and damaging wealth, and the bribe of 700,000 was proved by Li's confession during the investigation because he did not care about small anger and only cared about big things. However, because he voluntarily reported and confessed, a one-third reduction was made in accordance with the part of the criminal addition of the public servant, and the verdict of the main text was imposed. Chen Fumu's whereabouts were unknown, and another trial would be held when he was arrested. At this point, lawyer Jiang Yiping immediately appealed on behalf of Chen in court. The official advised that an appeal could be made to the Jiangsu Higher Court within ten days of receiving the verdict. Li was still not fully recovered from his illness and was sent back to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment.

Yesterday's High Tide Reached Over Thirty-Eight Feet in the Local Area

In recent days, the south wind has been strong, the rain has been drizzling, the weather has been warm, and the tide has been surging. Yesterday afternoon at 2 PM, the tide at Wusong Wenzao Creek was very high, level with the road, causing low-lying areas on the south bank to become flooded. According to customs officials, yesterday's tide rose to over thirty-eight feet, and the night tide was even higher. It is rare to have such a high tide in winter.

More Than Two Thousand Workers at Housheng Sue for Profit-Sharing, Negotiations Break Down

No Possibility of Reconciliation Between the Two Parties

Judge Orders Decision to be Announced on a Set Date

Since the Housheng Yarn Factory ceased operations, its staff and workers have repeatedly sued the factory's directors, Bei Runsheng and Xue Gansheng, in order to receive their share of the profits. For a year, Bei and Xue have been shuttling back and forth to court, with hardly a peaceful day. In the end, most cases were settled with compensation. However, as soon as one case was closed, another arose. Now, representatives Xu Guiquan, Wang Genxin, Chen Hongquan, Jin Jiajun, and others, claiming to represent 2,483 workers at Housheng, hired lawyers to demand that Bei and Xue share the profits, citing previous precedents. When they did not agree, they also filed a lawsuit for embezzlement in the First Special District Court. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qian Wenji opened the court to hear the case, and both plaintiffs and defendants arrived with their respective lawyers. Judge Qian first instructed the plaintiffs that the defendants had filed a counter-suit accusing them of making false accusations. Since you claim that you want to share the profits, you should provide proof. Xu Guiquan, upon hearing this, immediately stated that "Wan Heshang and others did the same work as us, and Wan and others have already received their share of the profits one after another, so we should receive the same treatment. We have letters from the workers' union that can prove it. We are all permanent workers," and so on. The plaintiffs' lawyer then explained the factory's employment system, saying that the factory's workers were divided into three types: monthly workers, daily workers, and temporary hires. The only difference between daily workers and monthly workers was that they were paid on a daily basis. Although the plaintiffs were all daily workers, many of them had worked for two or three years or more, so they should be considered permanent workers. As for whether they were entitled to a share of the profits, there had been too many lawsuits involving the factory's workers. Although some judgments had been dismissed, the results of each case had been that the workers received a share of the profits. The lawyer also cited the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau's mediation of a labor dispute involving workers at the South Railway Station as proof, saying that if the company had a surplus, 20% should be allocated to the workers as compensation. All Housheng workers had already received this share of the profits, so it would be unfair to exclude the plaintiffs. The defendants' lawyer also presented the Housheng Yarn Factory's articles of association, saying that even if there was a surplus, only the staff could share in it, not the workers. Moreover, since the plaintiffs were daily workers, their employment was temporary in nature, and they had no right to claim a share of the profits. Furthermore, the factory had no surplus at all. As for Wan Heshang Ji Weisan and others, they were only given some money after their lawsuit failed and during the January 28th Incident to help them return to their hometowns. Who knew that they would now be used as a pretext by the plaintiffs? It was truly difficult to do good deeds. The plaintiffs' lawyer then declared that Ji Weisan and others had reached a settlement outside of court and received seventy yuan each. Now, the plaintiffs only hoped to receive half that amount, thirty-five yuan each. Therefore, the plaintiffs' incidental civil suit was for a total of 86,950 yuan. The court then questioned the two defendants again. Because the two parties insisted on their own positions and there was no possibility of reconciliation, they ordered the lawyers from both sides to begin their arguments and concluded by ordering a decision to be announced on a set date.

Small-Scale Robbery Case Solved in Two Hours

Deda Rice Store Loses Over Eighty Yuan

Soap-Made Pistol and Stolen Goods Hidden in Socks

A robbery occurred near the Nanxiaonanmennei Yujialong area in the Southern District on the day before yesterday, around 5:00 PM. The victim was a rice store, which was robbed of over eighty silver dollars. The robbers then took the loot to the Desheng Restaurant on Xiangma Road and Wangmiao Street for dinner, where they were apprehended by the police. From the time of the robbery to the time the case was solved, only two hours had passed. Such speed was truly unexpected. The details of the case are recorded below: Xu Jiaren, a local resident, had been operating the Deda Rice Store at No. 171 Yujialong, Nanxiaonanmennei. On the day before yesterday, around 5:00 PM, two robbers suddenly came in, both around thirty years old, wearing blue cloth short shirts and pants. They broke into the store and each pulled out a pistol, threatening to make noise and shouting at the shop's accountant, "Where is the money?" At the time, the accountant saw the situation, knew that robbers had arrived, and was very frightened. He honestly answered that the money was in the cash register drawer. The robbers immediately opened the drawer and took all the silver dollars, over eighty yuan, and fled with the loot. The people in the store waited until the robbers had gone far away before calming down and reporting the incident to the 3rd Precinct of the 1st District, which had jurisdiction over the area, at 7:00 PM. After receiving the report, Chief Jin immediately used the telephone to report to the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the various district precincts, instructing them to pay attention to the investigation. Soon after, police chief Zhu Lianqing and police officers Shan Changyong and Dong Huaizhu from the 1st Precinct were patrolling the streets and passed by the Desheng Restaurant on Xiangma Road and Wangmiao Street. They noticed four men and a woman sitting together at a table inside the restaurant, eating heartily, but their behavior was suspicious. They immediately went inside and searched the group, but no contraband was found. When questioned about their origins, they were evasive. They were all taken to the station, where the chief interrogated them separately. Zhang Yiwen, 35 years old, from Yancheng, residing at No. 110 Laobaidu Street, confessed that this afternoon, he and his friends Li Jinsheng, Yong Jinbao, and Zhou Lianbao, the three arrested, met at a small teahouse in Lujiabang, bringing with them two pistols, one real and one fake. The real one he had bought from the front for forty yuan during the January 28 Incident. The fake one he had made from soap. At around 5:00 PM, they went to rob a rice store in Yujialong, Nanxiaonanmennei. Yong Jinbao and Zhou Lianbao waited outside as lookouts, while he and Li Jinsheng broke into the store. He pulled out the real pistol, and Li pulled out the fake pistol, threatening the people in the store to not make a sound, and they were able to rob them. After escaping with the loot, they went back to the small teahouse in Lujiabang, met up, and divided the loot. Li Jinsheng then called his mistress, Ma Gaoshi, and his mistress, Wu Zhoushi, the woman in the case, to come. He gave the real pistol to Ma Gaoshi to take back and hide, and he destroyed the fake pistol and threw it away by the side of the road. At that time, they saw that it was late, so they all entered the restaurant to fill their stomachs, when they were arrested by the police and brought to the station. Li Jinsheng, 34 years old, from Tongzhou, confessed that Ma Gaoshi had been his mistress for over ten years, and he was currently living with her at No. 45 Xie Xingli, Nanjing Street. The rest of his confession was the same as Zhang's. Yong Jinbao, 26 years old, from Gaoyou, confessed that the rest of his story was roughly the same as Zhang's. Zhou Lianbao, 32 years old, from Tongzhou, confessed that he lived in the same place as Li Jinsheng, and the rest of his story was the same as Zhang's. Wu Zhoushi, 25 years old, from Gaoyou, confessed that although she was Zhang's mistress, she really did not know about his actions outside. At the time, the police found twenty-two dollars and two cents of stolen money hidden on Zhou Yiwen's body, six dollars and four cents on Li Jinsheng's body, six dollars and one cent on Yong Jinbao's body, and four dollars and six cents on Zhou Lianbao's body. Most strangely, all of them had hidden the stolen money in their socks. They were ordered to be detained separately, and police officers were dispatched to Li Jinsheng's house to arrest his mistress, Ma Gaoshi, and his roommate, Chen Wushi, and interrogate them further. Ma Gaoshi, 51 years old, from Gaoyou, confessed that today, Zhang Yiwen had given her a pistol to take back, and she had immediately handed it over to his friend Xiao Wangzi to take out and hide. Chen Wushi, 32 years old, from Gaoyou, confessed that she lived with Ma Gaoshi and others, but she really did not know about their actions. Because the matter concerned robbery, it was ordered that the men and women be taken to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Charity Lottery Tickets Sell Well

The International Charity Horse Racing Special Prize Lottery Tickets, which have been selling in the local area recently, are selling very well because a free ticket is given for every ten tickets purchased at once, and the prize money is higher than that of ordinary champagne tickets. The banks, companies, newspapers, institutions, and organizations that sell the tickets are all very crowded. It is said that it is possible that they will be sold out soon. Recently, even small money shops on the streets, although not designated as sales agents, have been buying and reselling tickets. This is because the lottery tickets have a charitable nature, and promoting them is tantamount to helping a good cause. Moreover, there are many people who buy tickets individually, so it is possible to purchase ten tickets for one hundred yuan in cash from a sales agent, receive a free ticket (for a total of eleven tickets), and then resell them individually to obtain a considerable profit. If only ten tickets are sold, the remaining free ticket has a chance of winning a prize. It is possible to achieve multiple goals at once, so many people are happy to promote them.

Le Zhenbao Escapes Kidnapping; Is Thin and Weary

Le Was Bound All Over When Rescued

Nine Men and One Woman Captured in Bandit Den on Hart Road

Five Men and Two Women Further Arrested on Waterworks Street

Le Zhenbao, a Ningbo merchant in his sixties, has lived in Shanghai for decades and enjoys a high reputation among the Ningbo community. He owns the Taichang Furniture Company at 580 Nanjing Road and resides in his own residence on Yuyuan Road, where he keeps a car for transportation. On the morning of the 10th of this month, when Le was going to his company as usual, as his car approached the alley entrance, a group of kidnappers suddenly emerged from the roadside and abducted him. For nearly two weeks, there was no clue. Even in the last ten days, contact between the kidnappers and the family of the victim had been severed, leading to much speculation in society. It was widely believed that Mr. Le may have been harmed by the bandits, but this could not be confirmed. On the night of the 20th of this month, the French Concession police station on Rue Massenet discovered a telephone with suspicious gunshot sounds, and at the same time, contact between the kidnappers and Le's family ceased. Le's family was extremely worried, suspecting that the strange gunshot sound was related to Le's safety. However, rescue efforts continued unabated. To their surprise, the Old Zhabei Police Station received a tip the night before last that the kidnapped victim was being held in a bandit den at 911 Hart Road in the French Concession. Upon receiving the report, the head of the police station, along with all Chinese and foreign detectives, first contacted the special unit of the French Police and went to the address together at around 11:00 AM yesterday. They indeed captured nine male and one female kidnappers in the house, seizing three Mauser pistols, one handgun, and over five hundred rounds of ammunition. The kidnapped Le Zhenbao was rescued safely. However, Le's whole body was bound, and the suffering he endured in the bandit den was evident. When the detectives entered the house, one of the bandits attempted to escape through a window but was shot in the leg by a French Concession detective and captured. The bandit, named Wang Xiaoshizi, was immediately taken to the special unit and then transferred to the Old Zhabei Police Station. After the head of the police station interrogated each of them strictly, they confessed that other accomplices were hiding at 199 Waterworks Street in the French Concession. The police went to the address and arrested five more men and two women, who were taken into custody separately pending trial in court. The victim's family rushed to the scene upon hearing the news and found Le emaciated and exhausted. They immediately escorted him back to his residence. Reporters were unable to meet with him. As the police are still investigating this case, reporters were unable to inquire further. However, whether the strange gunshot sounds heard on the telephone were related to Le remains to be confirmed by Le in the future.

After the ceremony, the groomsman, bridesman, and officiant all gave speeches. The guests elected Director of Education Pan Gongzhan to deliver a speech on their behalf. The ceremony was solemn and grand, marking a momentous occasion. It is said that using the Chen Ying Shi Memorial Hall, a revolutionary martyr, as a wedding hall is a first.

Kidnapping Case Appeal: Defendants Retract Confessions

Zheng Shiying and Others Dissatisfied with the Previous Verdict

Qian Zhaofu, a native of Wuxi, and Pu Wenting were kidnapped by bandits in the French Concession last year. It was not until September of this year that Jin Jiulin, a detective of the special unit of the French Police, and others uncovered the kidnappers Zheng Shifan, Zhang Jiancheng, Zhang Afu, Gao Ada, and suspects Lu Liangqing and Zhao Xingsheng. The six individuals were handed over to the Second Special District Court, where the police lawyer filed a public prosecution in accordance with the law. Zheng Shifan and Zhang Afu were each sentenced to life imprisonment, Zhang Jiancheng was sentenced to fifteen years' imprisonment for each of two crimes, serving a total of twenty years, and Gao Ada was sentenced to fifteen years' imprisonment, with each being deprived of their civil rights. Lu and Zhao were found not guilty. It is now learned that the four convicts, Zheng and the others, were dissatisfied with the verdict and separately retained lawyers Zhao Zuwei, Wu Jingxiong, Qin Zemin, and Dong Yu to file an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court, upon receiving the appeal, summoned the entire case file, opened an investigative hearing, and concluded the inquiry. The High Court summoned the witnesses, Detective Zhang Ziying and Qin Youyu, and the victims, Qian Zhaofu and Pu Wenting, to the court yesterday afternoon. At 3:00 PM, Presiding Judge Zhou of the Criminal Court, along with Judges Guo and Zhu, together with Prosecutor Zhang Zongru, presided over the hearing in the Third Criminal Court. The police department was represented by lawyer Gu Shouxu. The defense lawyers retained by the appellants were also present. Court officials ordered bailiffs to bring the appellants from the detention center for questioning. Their testimonies were all changed from their initial confessions in the first trial. They denied the kidnapping and claimed they had been falsely accused, admitting only because they could not endure the torture, and requesting that justice be served. The hearing concluded at 5:00 PM. The court considered further investigation of evidence necessary and adjourned the hearing to a later date. The appellants were returned to custody.

Record of the Meeting of the Pengpu Security Corps

The Second Team of the Zhabei Pengpu Security Corps held a full team meeting at the team headquarters in Qiaoxing Lane, Datong Road, at around 3:00 PM yesterday. Approximately 100 people were present, including Team Leader Shangguan Rong, Platoon Leader Shi Yingfu, and section chiefs and team members from various defensive posts. After the customary rituals, the team leader first reported on the progress of events, followed by discussions on the following matters: 1) During the previous war in Zhabei, all team members retreated to Suzhou with the 19th Route Army, and their firearms were confiscated along the way. After the Japanese troops withdrew from Zhabei, the team headquarters prepared funds and sent personnel to the Wuxian District Office to retrieve a portion of Mauser pistols, rifles, etc. Upon inspection, the remaining firearms when the team retreated were all obsolete. With winter defense being critical and robberies occurring everywhere in recent days, carrying obsolete firearms for defense would not only be useless but also harmful. It was resolved to prepare a document and send Platoon Leader Shi Yingfu to the team headquarters, requesting that the funds for retrieving firearms from the Wuxian District Office be deducted from the winter defense funds. 2) The number of personnel on patrol each evening at 6:00 PM will be determined by the number of personnel at each defensive post, but there should be at least two to six people in each shift, rotating every three hours until 6:00 AM the next morning. In the event of local incidents, they will cooperate with the security team and the police. 3) Yang Xialing, a member of the Tangqiao District Security Corps in Pudong, previously opened fire while patrolling at night and killed Jiang Guohua, a petitioner police officer from the municipal government, when checking pedestrians. Although the case has been handled by the Shanghai Local Court, a verdict has not yet been reached. Upon receiving letters from various sectors in Pudong requesting assistance, the team decided to express its support by waiting for the court's verdict, first sending someone to comfort Mr. Yang, and then preparing a document to submit to the Reorganization Committee, seeking assistance. Finally, other matters were discussed, which were not of significant importance and were omitted. The meeting adjourned at 6:15 PM.

Two Stores Robbed Simultaneously

Robbery Case on Qiqihaer Road

Over Ten Shots Fired Upon Leaving

Yu Chang South Goods Store at 901 Taihe Street, Qiqihaer Road, Gaolang Bridge, Yangshupu, and Rui Xingren Rice Store across the street at 93-97, were simultaneously robbed by five bandits last night at 6:30 PM. Three bandits broke into the Rui Xingren Rice Store, while two entered the Yu Chang South Goods Store, threatening with guns and wantonly looting. As a result, Yu Chang Store was robbed of a total of 288 yuan in cash and small denomination notes. Rui Xingren Rice Store was robbed of over 300 yuan. As they left, fearing the shop staff would chase after them, they fired over ten shots into the air, fleeing towards the northeast. Afterwards, the shop owners reported the incident to the Yangshupu Police Station, requesting an investigation.

Souls Under the Wheels

Rickshaw Passenger: At around 8:30 AM yesterday morning, near the western end of Mingfu Lane, North Nicheng Bridge, Xinzha Road, a No. 15046 Route 10 public bus sped past, and a Mr. Jia, about thirty years old, wearing a black robe, riding a rickshaw, was coming face-to-face. Unable to avoid it in time, he was knocked to the ground, his head severely crushed, and he died instantly. The police rushed to the scene upon hearing the news, recorded the bus number, and sent the body to Renji Hospital to await autopsy.

Rickshaw Puller: Huang Shou, a native of Tongzhou, 52 years old, worked as a rickshaw puller. The other day in the afternoon, while pulling rickshaw No. 3974, he was traveling south to north on Yunnan Road, near the Zhifu Road tram tracks, when the shaft of a rickshaw pulled by Ji Zicheng suddenly pierced the wheel of Huang's rickshaw, causing it to crash. Huang fell onto the tram tracks, and at that moment, tram No. 61 of Route 3, driven by Guo Peigong, was approaching. Before Guo could stop, the tram ran over Huang, causing serious injuries. He was sent to Renji Hospital but died despite treatment. The body was sent to the Fei Lun Road Mortuary. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court appointed Prosecutor Liang Ce to the scene for inspection. It was determined that the deceased, Huang Shou, male, died from being hit by the tram. The investigation revealed that rickshaw puller Ji Zicheng was at fault, and the police should investigate and send him to the court for processing. The body was released to his brother, Huang Quan, for funeral arrangements.

Municipal Finance Bureau Issues Notice on Tax Exemption Standards for Handwoven Cloth

Technical Improvements in Handwoven Cloth

The Standard of the Sixteenth Year of the Republic Is No Longer Applicable

The Municipal Finance Bureau issued a notice to the Business Tax Collection Office of this city, forwarding a directive from the Executive Yuan, based on a joint submission from the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, regarding the standard for uniform tax exemption for handwoven cloth. The directive stated, in brief, "Based on the instructions, the standard for handwoven cloth set by the Hubei Province, regardless of whether it is made of natural-colored cotton yarn, foreign yarn, or woven by hand looms or iron looms, is uniformly limited to three feet in length and one foot two inches to one foot six inches in width. It is further reported that the submission is based on the precedent for handwoven cloth tax exemption prior to the sixteenth year of the Republic, which seems to refer to the standard for handwoven cloth set by the former Beijing government in the seventh year of the Republic. However, currently, handwoven cloth has undergone considerable technical improvements to meet social needs, which often conflict with the previous standard. Since various regions have followed your esteemed Yuan's clear directive to exempt handwoven cloth from business tax, the exemption measures also vary greatly and should be unified for compliance. Having consulted with both ministries and considered the precedent of the seventh year of the Republic and the supply and demand of handwoven cloth in various regions, a new standard is proposed: 1) It must be woven by hand-operated looms, hand-pulled looms, or foot-operated looms. 2) It is limited to plain weave and twill weave, but striped or checkered plain weave or twill weave are included. 3) Whether it is handspun yarn or machine-spun yarn, the single yarn must not exceed 20 counts, and the double-strand yarn must not exceed 16 counts. 4) There are no restrictions on width or length. 5) There are no restrictions on original color or dyeing. The above five items are proposed to be submitted to your esteemed Yuan for review and to be circulated to all provinces and cities for compliance, without the need to follow the six tax exemption standards for handwoven cloth set in the seventh year of the Republic. All reasons for the directive to review the Hubei Province's standard for handwoven cloth should be followed. Whether this is appropriate, we respectfully submit this document for review and instructions, etc. It should be approved and circulated for compliance."

Cotton Inspection Fee Collected at Six Fen per Dan

Regardless of Export or Domestic Sale

Implemented on New Year's Day

The Second National Commodity Inspection Conference resolved that the cotton inspection fee would be uniformly collected at six fen per dan, regardless of export or domestic sale. The resolution has been submitted to and approved by the Ministry of Industry, and it will be implemented starting on January 1, 1933. The Ministry has ordered commodity inspection bureaus in various regions to comply. The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau has been ordered to comply and will change the collection starting on January 1 next year. It has been announced in the newspapers for all Chinese and foreign cotton merchants to be informed.

The Three Telegraph Bureaus' Labor Dispute; Party and Government to Discuss Measures

The Company Will Conduct Direct Negotiations Today

Xin Sheng News Agency reported that the strike by messengers at the Great Northern, Great Eastern, and Pacific Telegraph Bureaus has not been resolved despite mediation from various parties. In order to avoid the expansion of the labor dispute and affect local security, the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau have decided to consult again on concrete measures to resolve the issue as soon as possible. Chinese directors such as Yu Qiaqing are prepared to take the lead in trying to mediate. As for the three companies using Western directors to perform delivery work, which is insufficient for Chinese workers, there have been many letters of complaint, which has greatly affected the company's credibility and future prospects. Special senior Chinese staff have been entrusted to contact the workers. There is generally hope for a return to work. According to the Trade Union of Western Merchants' Telegraph Delivery Industry in the Third District, the labor and management sides may conduct direct negotiations today.

Lawyer Fang Junjie is the son of the late Shen Shidianying of Qingpu. He graduated from the College of Law and Politics. The Four Banks Issuance Preparation Report

No. 156

The Four Banks Reserve, jointly established by the Yien Yieh, Kincheng, China & South Sea and Continental Banks, is dedicated to the issuance of China & South Sea Bank notes. In accordance with the Bank's issuance regulations, banknotes are fully backed by reserves, with cash reserves accounting for at least 60% and guarantee reserves accounting for up to 40%. It is announced once a week, and audited by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The 156th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve on December 24, 1932, is recorded as follows: Total banknote circulation: $24,798,657; Total reserves: $24,798,657; including Cash reserves: $18,894,157; Guarantee reserves: $5,900,500.

How to Solve the Problem of Coexistence Between Men and Women - Mr. Li Junsheng's Question

I am not qualified to talk about the issue of coexistence between men and women. Logically speaking, although I am in my twenties, I have never been intimate with a woman in this charming and colorful Shanghai. Therefore, I consider myself unqualified to discuss this issue. When I say this, the general readers may scold me for wanting to eat cold pork head, pretending to be a moralist, but that is not the case. To be honest, I am a little timid. Why? First, I am just a small employee in a foreign firm, with a monthly income of only forty or fifty dollars. My monthly expenses are roughly as follows: rent eight dollars, food twelve dollars, transportation five dollars, nanny for cleaning toilets and washing clothes two dollars, barber and washing three dollars. My family has an elderly mother, and I have to send at least ten dollars or so every month. In this way, "the money is earned with sweat," and there is no surplus at all. If you get sick, take medicine, and hire a doctor, there is no way out, only one pawn (verb) pawn (noun!). This is still a minor illness. If a major illness comes, first, it will drag on for days, and problems will arise in the company. Second, medicine is so expensive that it cannot last, not only will the illness not get better, but there will be no food to eat, and there will only be one way to die. There is no need to think about the problem of men and women. Second, my experience warns me not to get involved in this issue. Because a relative of mine was a returned student from the West, and had a doctorate in literature. However, he was too loyal and did not know how to "drill holes," and his strange ideas were out of date. Therefore, although he had good qualifications, solid knowledge, gentle temperament, and a bright and upright attitude, I often thought that if I were a girl, I would desperately love him and help him succeed in a kind of learning, but he was ultimately "cheated" once because of a woman! His spirit was greatly hit. The thing is like this: there is a new-style woman, the so-called "fashion" girl, she is not only a modern girl on the surface, but also has been to the most modern school, to the most modern place, and also holds the most modern signboard in her thoughts. When she had not found other more suitable men, she once combined with my relative, the Doctor. My relative bought her fur coats, high-heeled shoes, and socks for two dollars a pair. He never put his feet in the game of lust, but for her sake, the Doctor had to often accompany her to the Paris Ballroom, the Central Grand Theater, and the Carlton. This modern girl seemed to be satisfied temporarily. However, "the sky has unpredictable winds and clouds, and people have misfortunes and blessings." His friend was sued in Hong Kong, and the Doctor, eager to help others, immediately ran to Hong Kong to rescue his friend, and this modern girl took the opportunity to go to Beiping to visit relatives. By the time the Doctor returned from Hong Kong, he found that the house was empty and there was no news. After a long time, he learned that this modern girl had met a more agreeable man in Beiping, who was not only rich but also an official, and often ate "champagne!" with foreigners. You think, even my Doctor relative, who is such a person, is inevitably deceived by a modern girl. What qualifications do I, a small employee, have to deal with those modern Misses? I can only sigh! However, people are always made of flesh, and they always have sexual problems. After finishing work, he feels the loneliness of the world, and in social situations, he feels the loneliness of life. This is really a painful thing! I am lucky that your reporter has taught me!

Answer: Reading your letter, my heart is pounding. I hate that I am not God, who can create thousands of affectionate and kind women in the seven days of creating the world, so that "all lovers in the world can become married!" However, this is just a joke, not a solution to the problem. The following is "getting back to the point." 1. Your salary is low, to be honest, you are not qualified to marry a modern Miss. If you want to "a toad wants to eat swan meat," then you are not only "climbing a tree to catch a fish," but also "doing nothing good, but harming yourself." Don't be delusional. If a modern woman really patronizes you, then you can only learn to "sit in meditation like an old monk" and close the door to visitors. 2. Don't panic when you hear this. This is not teaching you to really become a monk and cut off worldly ties. "Heroes still seek in the grass." Find a loyal and simple woman in the dust or in a small family to be friends with, but be sure to find a way to avoid childbirth. 3. The incident of your relative Doctor is a common occurrence in modern society, and is not surprising. Modern women are products of urban life. In modern society, they pursue the entertainment of one-sided material life all day long: dancing, movies, modern clothes and shoes, the trembling and temptation of the flesh, the pursuit of money and power. This is an inevitable phenomenon of "leisure society," that is, a few who have superficially received a little new-style education, or even received revolutionary education. These women are even worse. They are just "hanging sheep's heads and selling dog meat," and satisfying their carnal desires under the smokescreen of mechanical materialism, not "purely hedonistic" materialism. They also often say a few theories that are "donkey lips not matching horse mouths," what "freedom," what "oppression," and even what "ism," to defend themselves. In fact, they are "the drunkard's intention is not in the wine." Their purpose is very simple, that is: "enjoyment! enjoyment!" This is not an accidental thing! It is the phenomenon that a group of owners in the real society is declining day by day. Let us take this opportunity to give them a death knell!

The fall of modern women! Fall! Fall quickly!

Famous doctors at sea were invited, but to no avail, and her condition became more critical. Recently, a friend introduced her to He Shuying, a master of acupuncture, for a diagnosis. Letters

Letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction

Dear Sir, I have read a dispatch from Wuhu in your newspaper on the 25th of this month, which briefly stated that the long-distance buses on the western section of the Jing-Wu Road have been approved by the Anhui Provincial Department of Construction and will be open to traffic on January 1, 1933. Although the eastern section has also been submitted by merchants to organize a company, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction has been picky and unwilling to sign a contract, resulting in the failure of traffic between the two places, which not only hinders transportation, but also seems to violate the intention of building the road. The western section of the long-distance bus company has reported to the Provincial Chamber of Commerce to submit to the Anhui Provincial Department of Construction for consultation with this department to quickly recruit merchants to undertake the project to facilitate transportation. This department has approved the application of Shi Yudian, director of the Preparatory Committee of the Jing-Wu Road Eastern Section Long-Distance Bus Company, and deputy directors Wang Yaojiu and Sun Haimin, to operate long-distance buses on the eastern section of the Jing-Wu Road in accordance with all the methods of the Anhui Provincial Department of Construction, and is currently negotiating the draft contract. Shi Yudian, the director of the Preparatory Committee of the company, also stated that since the route includes the area under the jurisdiction of the Beijing Municipal Government, can a terminal be set up within the scope of the municipal government after business begins? If it is necessary to divide the boundary, the starting point should be Andemen in Jiangning County, which is far from the city, and business will definitely be affected. In addition, the original share capital is not much, and funds are needed everywhere for purchasing vehicles and equipment. If the municipal government allows the establishment of a station, or it is necessary to prepay donations and taxes, I am afraid that it will be difficult to turn around. At this time, if the share capital is increased, it is also the time when the abolition of the lunar calendar is not far away, and finance is extremely tight, and it is difficult to raise funds. For the sake of prudence, Yudian and others have repeatedly gathered all the colleagues to consider in detail, and they all believe that it is impossible to handle. If it delays the future, it is better to stop the process to avoid future troubles. It is reasonable to declare the situation and ask the director to approve the cancellation of the case to end the matter. The case has been approved for cancellation. The eastern section of the Jing-Wu Road Long-Distance Bus is that the merchant himself is unwilling to undertake it, and it is not that this department is picky and unwilling to sign a contract. The reports of the western section of the long-distance bus company are inconsistent with the facts. In addition to finding another way to recruit merchants to undertake the project, and informing the Anhui Provincial Department of Construction for investigation, the corresponding letter is requested to be published in your newspaper to clarify the truth. Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction, December 26.

Important News

Chen Bu Lei Talks About Education Reform By Following the Trend

Rumors That I Will Head the Ministry of Education Are Inaccurate

Chen Bu Lei, member of the Central Committee and Director of Education of Zhejiang Province, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. Chen at his residence yesterday to inquire about his views on education reform and the recent situation in Zhejiang Province. According to Mr. Chen, the modern education system does need to be reformed. Mr. Chen Guofu proposed a very practical education reform plan at the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee. However, this plan is not an improvement plan, but a revolutionary plan. The current school system must be completely changed. Therefore, it cannot be realized in a short time and must go through a considerable preparation time before it can be implemented. The Jingdian [Beijing Telegraph] rumor that I will head the Ministry of Education is completely inaccurate. I will stay in Shanghai for about two or three days and then return to Hangzhou.

Books Not Meeting New Standards Returned for Revision and Review

The National Compilation and Translation Bureau, following the Ministry of Education's order to adhere to the newly announced curriculum standards when reviewing textbooks for primary and secondary schools, and to submit unreviewed materials to the Ministry for return, has taken the following action: In addition to reviewing textbooks submitted by various publishing houses after the announcement of the curriculum based on the new standards, a separate list of materials submitted to the Bureau previously that have not been fully reviewed or not yet reviewed has been submitted to the Ministry of Education. The Ministry has been requested to instruct the respective publishing houses to revise them according to the officially announced standards and resubmit them for review. Opening of the Shandong Education Bureau Chiefs' Meeting

Jinan, 26th (Telegraph) - The Provincial Education Bureau Chiefs' Meeting of the second session opened this morning, the 26th. The Director of Education, He Siyuan, chaired the meeting and reported on the progress of education in the province over the past year. The number of primary school students has increased from 670,000 to 1,090,000. However, a major mistake in past education was that education was separated from the occupations of those receiving it and could not support production. In the future, reforms should be carried out urgently. The first step is to passively enable those receiving education to be content with their existing lives, and the second step is to actively enable them to assist in household production. In the afternoon, a discussion was held.

Wuxi, Jiangsu Provincial Education Institute, in order to promote art and respect the art of Mr. Liu Haisu, repeatedly requested Mr. Liu to lend more than one hundred points of Chinese and Western works. From December 28 to January 3, they will be exhibited publicly in the Wuxi urban area county library, county education association and the institute to allow the public to have an opportunity to appreciate art, thereby opening up the inland atmosphere. In the past two days, Liu's Chinese and Western paintings have been transported to Wuxi, and Mr. Han Juejian and Mr. Song Banggan are responsible for the layout. Nankai Principal Zhang Boling Assaulted

Ordered by the Ministry of Education to expel students...due to student dissatisfaction.

Tianjin, 27th (Telegraph) - Nankai School, under a secret order from the Ministry of Education, expelled more than 30 students on the 25th and more than 20 students on the 27th. All of them had distinct political leanings, so the reasons for the expulsion were not announced. The students were dissatisfied and assaulted Principal Zhang Boling, causing his head to bleed. They also destroyed the principal's office. The Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched special agents to the school for protection.

Special Article

A Sincere Appeal to University and Middle School Students Nationwide to Practice National Salvation Through Education (7) by You Huaigao

(7) Universal Rural Education

Method: It is said that China has 1,911 counties, approximately 1 million villages, with an average of 500 villages per county, including 100 large villages. Now, let's start with the large villages. If each county has 200 university or middle school graduates who, after graduating, spend a year teaching the children of farmers in the countryside, at least 30 million children could immediately receive education. Each county has 100 large villages, and 2,000 counties have 200,000 villages. If each village has two teachers teaching 150 children, that's 30 million children. As the number of university and middle school students increases each year, the number of teachers will also increase, so the number of children receiving education will also increase. On the one hand, university and middle school students will voluntarily implement education, starting the trend. On the other hand, the government will raise educational funds widely and promote education. Five years later, among the tens of millions of educated rural children, at least several million will be qualified to become rural teachers. Ten years later, education can be popularized. This is the method of popularizing education.

Responsibility: When I go to the countryside and see farmers in coarse clothing and simple food, even farmers lacking food and clothing, I don't feel particularly sad because this is the result of our ancestors not knowing how to educate farmers. However, when I see countless innocent and lively young compatriots surrounding me, I feel very sad because if we still don't think about teaching them, they will grow up to be the poor farmers of China in the future. Therefore, we have a great mission and responsibility towards this group of children.

Career: Look at the remoteness of the northwestern provinces, and then look at Xinjiang, Mongolia, Tibet, Xikang, Qinghai, Suiyuan, and other places with large amounts of undeveloped land. If there are traces of university and middle school students everywhere, then your careers will never end. This is a very large task for you beyond rural education. Therefore, you are also creators of opening up wasteland and relocating farmers. Furthermore, the major domestic banks are currently trying to circulate a portion of their capital in rural areas, and the government is also working hard to use economics to solve the decline of rural areas. Therefore, after you arrive in the countryside, you will be financial agents. So, in the countryside, you are not only a teacher, military advisor, doctor, and engineer, but also an agriculturalist, economist, politician, and creator. The countryside is a single cell, and you are the nucleus of life in that single cell. In the future, the preservation and development of that cell depends on you. To put it simply, you are the village chief of a village because it's not just about teaching a few primary school students to recognize characters and read a few books, it's because other responsibilities are extremely important. This important mission cannot be fulfilled by ordinary rural teachers, so I specially and solemnly ask university and middle school students nationwide to take on the role of teachers. I am still afraid that their knowledge is insufficient, so I want to ask specialized talents nationwide to organize associations to broadcast teaching materials and implementation methods daily via radio.

Hope: Therefore, the policies of national salvation that you previously paraded and shouted for in the cities can be transformed into a policy of national salvation that educates and progresses in the countryside because the audience in the cities, even if they are enthusiastic and patriotic, is only a temporary emotional impulse, which ultimately becomes empty. Because they are not your believers, they cannot absorb your profound meanings. Therefore, I ask you to return to the countryside to cultivate your believers who can truly sacrifice for the country. If every university and middle school student can cultivate ten believers, after five years, the country can obtain millions of young vanguards for national salvation. I am afraid that at this time, you will find the filth and ugliness within the concessions to be disgusting and terrifying, and you will be willing to build your new-style Peach Blossom Spring, a scientific and electrified small Shanghai, with your believers and your lovers according to your ideals. This is my sincere and earnest hope for the success of your future in rural education. You are still in your youth or prime of life, and you can still see the ideal Republic of China that you have created with your own eyes.

Success: Therefore, the realization of this ideal and the success of this career depend entirely on you holding a sacrificial spirit of sacrificing for the country, a patriotic spirit of enduring hardship and adversity, a humanitarian spirit of a religious figure, and an adventurous spirit of an explorer. With this spirit, you can save the country, you can resist foreign aggression. Going to work in the countryside, you will have hardship to endure, you will have adversity to taste, and only then will you get the true meaning of ten years of accumulation and ten years of education. This educational service should be regarded as serious as military service, and the current important work should be regarded as urgent as facing the enemy in a serious battle. The farmers are treated as beasts of burden, suffering injustice. You should be their ladder, helping them ascend to the ranks of the masters and share human happiness. You should respect their parents as your own parents, and love their children as your own children. You must solve their livelihoods, and you must relieve their hardships. You must at least temporarily forget about rewards and say goodbye to money, forget about all the glory and wealth. You must know that this is our rare and evil era, this is our critical moment of life and death. We are currently few in number and weak in strength, and we are being bullied by others. Therefore, we must go separately to call for reinforcements, and we must spend ten years cultivating them, cultivating them to be worthy of being our national salvation helpers. As for the bandits in the interior, they were never born to be bandits. They were originally good farmers, so you must not have a timid and hesitant heart. You should accept the guidance of the association and the success of the government, which is also the success of national salvation through education.

Tong, Lou Tang, Xiang Gong, Feng Lu, Kuishan, and Xu Hang schools. Local News

Municipal Education Bureau Prohibits Extending Holidays

The Municipal Education Bureau has determined that the dates for the annual holidays for primary and secondary schools in the 21st year of the Republic are to begin on January 1, 22nd year of the Republic and end on January 2nd, 22nd year of the Republic, and the winter holidays are to begin on January 24th, 22nd year of the Republic and end on January 31st, 22nd year of the Republic. These dates have already been established and schools have been notified to comply. Recently, it has been heard that a small number of private schools are preparing to start their holidays early or extend their holidays, which is detrimental to the studies of young students. Yesterday, the Bureau specifically ordered all schools to strictly comply with the holiday dates stipulated in the school calendar and not to start early or extend, in order to comply with the advice.

Results of the Boy Scout Aircraft Fundraising

First Fundraising Exceeds 3,000 Yuan

Aviation General Organization to Continue

The City Boy Scout Council, in view of the importance of aviation to national salvation, originally scheduled to mobilize on December 3rd and 4th to raise funds for the Boy Scout aircraft. However, the municipal government instructed the City Boy Scout Council to postpone the event because the Aviation General Organization was not yet ready. Therefore, the first fundraising effort has temporarily come to an end. Statistics show that more than 2,000 members were recruited and over 3,166.07 yuan were raised. The funds are currently signed jointly by Yin Zhiling of the Aviation Construction Association and Zhu Jiahua of the City Boy Scout Council and deposited in Xinhua Bank as the China Boy Scout Aircraft Fund. After the Aviation General Organization is established, fundraising will continue. It is reported that the groups with the most fundraising achievements were Southeast Women's Physical Education College, Guangong, Fudan, Ningbo No. 1, Shanghai Middle School, Guanghua, Moore Hall, Huizhong, and East Asia. It is also reported that the 24th Standing Committee Meeting of the Aviation Construction Association decided to award a medal to all Boy Scouts who participated in this campaign.

Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Institute of Engineers

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Institute of Engineers held its December regular meeting at 6:00 PM yesterday (the 26th) at the Banking Association at No. 3 Hong Kong Road. 29 people including Mr. Wang Erzhou attended. First, they had a dinner together, then the President of the Association, Mr. Xu Peihuang, delivered an opening speech and discussed the preparation for the New Year's Eve party next year. Mayo, consultant of the Ministry of Railways, gave a speech on "My Opinions on Chinese Railways," stating that he came to China to investigate the Chinese railway industry and found that its progress was very rapid and very different from what he had heard. If it can be gradually improved, it will not be difficult to be on par with Europe and the United States. Finally, Mr. Zhang Huikang, a member of the Association, gave a speech on "The Structure and Application of Red Neon Lights in a Year." He said that the manufacturing method of red neon lights and its application are completely based on the theory of electricity, and he carried red neon application equipment and demonstrated it on the spot, which was very interesting. The meeting adjourned after 9:00 PM.

Chi Zhi quickly caught up, and by the end of the first half, Chi Zhi was only behind by three points at 24 to 27. At the start of the second half, Chi Zhi tied the score at 34 to 34. Due to Ren Jiexing being penalized out, Chi Zhi took the lead at 38 to 35. However, Xia Guang then scored six consecutive points, reversing the score to 41 to 38. The situation became very tense. Xia Guang's defense ultimately secured a 49 to 41 victory.

You You Held the Advantage in the First Half

The Shanghai Football Club (S.H.C.), once a team with a cloud of talented players and a commanding presence on the Shanghai scene, has seen its strength sharply decline in recent years due to the passage of time, the retirement of talent, and a lack of successors. Free Talk

Massage

— Ms. Lu Yin

It's Saturday afternoon again. Xiao Bo leaned lazily on the sofa, looking at the bright autumn sun outside the window, and said to his wife in a crooked voice, "Oh, this boring life is really too boring."

"Do you want to go somewhere to play?" his wife asked softly.

"Yes, ah, you think someone has worked for six days, and it's not too uncomfortable if you don't find a way to enjoy it on Saturday afternoon?" Xiao Bo still said complainingly.

"Then where are you talking about going?"

"I want to go see dancing."

"Of course, it's okay to watch dancing, but neither of us can dance. It's not very interesting to be a fool there!"

Hearing his wife's words, Xiao Bo felt even more unhappy, and quickly sat up straight, saying in a more serious tone, "You're always like this, you don't want to go here, and you don't want to go there. We don't get along very well on this point. I extremely like activities, but you are like a rotten log, wanting to hide at home all day long. Alas. We simply don't get along very well."

Seeing Xiao Bo's red-faced and bulging-necked appearance, his wife felt a little uncomfortable, so she said with a sneer, "Originally, it's rare to find someone in the world who can be the same in everything, unless one of them completely erases their personality and takes other people's interests as their own, and takes other people's will as their own. This way, they can be the same. Otherwise, even twin brothers born to the same parents will have some minor differences. It's natural to be different, what's so strange about it!"

"I think we should go our separate ways every Saturday in the future!" Xiao Bo thought for a while and said this.

"There's nothing wrong with that. I never want to force you to spend time with me. If you think I sometimes hinder your behavior, then just do as you please!" his wife said somewhat angrily and went downstairs. So, a beautiful autumn afternoon passed sadly in their anger.

On Tuesday afternoon, Xiao Bo returned from teaching at school... It was already late, and his wife quickly approached and asked, "Why are you coming home at this time today?"

"Oh," Xiao Bo responded absently, and leaned on the sofa to think deeply.

"What's wrong with you, acting so strangely?" his wife said with a smile, while stroking his forehead with her hand, "Are you sick?"

Xiao Bo raised his eyelids and looked at his wife with those dreamy, mysterious eyes. After a long, long time, he said in a low voice, "I'm very sad today... There's something I didn't want to tell you, but it's uncomfortable to keep it in my heart, so I'll tell you anyway!"

"What is it? Tell me! You don't have to hide anything from me!" his wife said with a smile.

"Yesterday, I went to a massage parlor!"

"Why go for a massage, are you sick?"

"You're really a fool, would someone who is sick go to a massage parlor to die?"

"Then what do you do at the massage parlor?"

"I went to have fun."

Excluding Geniuses

— Qi Fan

I don't want to quote the views of the Italian criminologist Cesare Lombroso, who sees geniuses as a kind of mentally ill person, a kind of madman whose mental powers are not balanced, and should be excluded. Geniuses should be excluded, not because they are mentally ill and can be given some leniency, nor because they are not mentally ill and should be praised. The only reason is that geniuses are different from us ordinary people. In our vulgar society, we don't need any geniuses, so we want to exclude them.

The vast majority of people in our society are mediocre people, ordinary people, absolutely not geniuses in any aspect. We mediocre people have our own way of life, our own path, and we don't need geniuses who are different from us mediocre people to guide and lead us. Geniuses only know their own way of life and the path of geniuses, which is useless in our vulgar society. We no longer dare to hope that everyone will become a genius and use the way of life of geniuses and take the path of geniuses. It is an unforgivable mistake for ordinary people to take the path of geniuses.

In fact, the history of this kind of mistake is too long. In the past, our mediocre and foolish ancestors followed geniuses, forgetting their own path. Geniuses took it upon themselves to be the leaders of the masses, and the masses seemed to be unable to move an inch without a genius leader. This error lies in the fact that the masses do not take their own path but take the path of geniuses. The masses forgot that they had their own path and followed geniuses to conquer the country, seize the world, and support a tyrannical emperor, sacrificing millions of lives and heads. The successful ones are geniuses, the sacrificed ones are the masses, so we can know that the masses have not done what they should have done. On the contrary, the farmers who till the land and the craftsmen who build houses, although they have not built any great achievements, give us food and houses, and we are truly blessed.

The first thing to do is to recognize what our common people need? What we want is not the title of chief or committee member, nor amazing achievements and feats, let alone certificates and commendations. What we want is nothing more than a peaceful life, enough food, clothing, and shelter. We do not hope for complete enjoyment, nor do we want to see compatriots who are naked and starving. We cannot all be rich and powerful, so we do not hope to be. We are mediocre people, and we are satisfied if we can all have the same life. We want to exclude those who, like geniuses, hope to sit above the masses. We absolutely do not hope to be better than others, to stand out from others. The guideline of our ordinary people lies in universal equality.

If someone says that we have no ambition to improve, yes, that is the essence of the life of our ordinary people. No competition, no desire to be superior, no desire to abandon our own vocation, is the golden rule of our ordinary people. We take the smooth road, not the ladder to heaven. We do not seek honor, and we avoid humiliation. In short, we ordinary people can only do ordinary things, and cannot follow others to do things above ordinary.

Geniuses are different from us ordinary people. They have the ambition to improve, they want to climb to heaven, they want to lead a group of people to make great achievements, they want people to follow them for a great cause, but they are unwilling to do it alone. They often want to lure ordinary people to agree and support them. They want to blame ordinary people for not supporting him, not worshiping him, they want to enjoy the sacrifice of ordinary people, they want to suck the blood of ordinary people, they want to be the leader of ordinary people, but they do not give ordinary people the slightest benefit. Therefore, geniuses are the enemies of our ordinary people. We are ordinary people, and we want to exclude geniuses, whether they are geniuses at killing people, geniuses at plundering, geniuses at cheating, geniuses at boasting, or even geniuses at eating and shitting, we must exclude them.

X X X X

Random Jottings from Wuxiang Hermitage

— Shi Zhecun

Last night, I read Tang Yuansu's "Chronicle of a Journey to the West in the Gengzi Year," which recorded a Boxer Rebellion incantation: "First bow, the gates of heaven open; second bow, the earth's portals crack; third, summon Sun Wukong; fourth, summon Zhu Bajie." It is said that this incantation was very effective, and a young child who possessed it could defeat a strong man. Another incantation to ward off cannon fire read: "Water freezes mountains, ice freezes caves, in the ice cave there is an ice man." All of this is bizarre and worthy of a chuckle.

It also records an essay, an argument, and a poem topic from Hong Xiuquan's imperial examinations: the essay topic was: "Confusing words from a crooked plate, red water floods the world, God's eternal covenant, the curved sun's teachings." The argument topic was: "Filial piety to parents, filial piety to grandfather." The poem topic was: "Seeking fish, one obtains Wu; like a starving man seeking rice and obtaining Rong. Five-character, eight-line verse, rhyme unrestricted." The "grandfather" in the argument topic probably refers to Christ, and the character "Wu" in the poem topic is suspected of being an error, but the essay topic is completely incomprehensible.

Kuang Zhouyi's Jinqian lyrics, Wanghaichao Jiang Jianxia assigned the topic of a portrait of a Japanese girl, Xiao Hua, with a note citing a Japanese proverb: "Shinshu buckwheat, lover's handsome face, not eating buckwheat is still alright, but missing my lover makes me worried," with a charm similar to reading Qu songs at midnight. I wonder what the original text was like.

When an author has a new book published, they often like to personally sign their name and send it to relatives and friends. French writers who are not in Paris, when they have a new book out, will include a business card with the inscription: "Respectfully presented by so-and-so, who is not in Paris," to make it clear that they were unable to personally sign it. As for the novelist Paul Morand, who travels the world, he would often print: "Respectfully presented by Morand, far from Europe." The president of the Writers' Association, Claude Farrère, recently gave away his new book, "L'Atlantique en rond," with a business card that read: "Respectfully presented by Farrère, who cannot sign by hand." It is said that when Gogoloff attempted to assassinate President Doumer, Farrère suffered collateral damage and his hand was injured, hence this unique presentation inscription.

Years ago, during the war between Qi and Lu, I took refuge in Shanghai and walked along Jing'an Temple Road at night, composing a quatrain: "A graceful jade moon rises, leaning on the vast and lonely army with a cold glow; late at night, it flows into Jin City, yet illuminates the dancing girls returning on Silver Street." Today, rereading it, I think it is quite suitable to be sung about the Northeast.

Impressions of Suzhou (II)

— Zhenfu

We went further inside and saw many historical sites, including the Sword Testing Stone of the King of Wu, which is split in the middle, and the remains of Zhen Niang. Further inside, there is a sloping stone ground with various wrinkles on the stone, but no cracks can be found. This stone ground is about five or six zhang square, like a large stone, naturally formed like this. It is said that the tomb of the King of Wu is buried in the middle of the stone, which is of course a mythological folk legend. On the stone wall, there are large characters of "Tiger Hill" by Yan Zhenqing, with very majestic brushstrokes. Further in from the left, there is the so-called Sword Pond, surrounded by stone walls, with vines and wisteria winding around the stones. The water in the pond is dark green, and the sunlight can only penetrate through the branches and leaves of the vines and wisteria, so it is inevitably gloomy, as if one has reached the deep mountains where no one lives, and has become another world.

We walked to the top of Tiger Hill, where there are several new-style buildings, small bridges, cement roads, halls, pavilions, and so on. To the left of the new-style buildings, there are dilapidated walls and broken tiles, and a desolate ancient pagoda, with the golden paint peeling off, which has become a comfortable nest for birds. The new and old aspects complement each other interestingly. In addition, there are treasure halls, monks' rooms, and many imperial steles of Qianlong, which are commonly found in famous temples everywhere. When we came down from Tiger Hill, on the left side of the road, there was a cave made of stacked stones, said to have been built by Xi Shi to avoid the invasion of King Goujian of Yue. Such folk legends are actually taken seriously and built. The curiosity of the people of Suzhou can be imagined.

In Tiger Hill, there is also a kind of person who specializes in leading tourists, pointing out historical sites, and telling legends about them. Among these people, I think many folk legends must be preserved, although there is a suspicion that they have been embellished and fabricated. However, if someone can record them, it may be a good reference material for studying folk stories.

In Tiger Hill, we learned about the historical sites of Suzhou and how the people of Suzhou are fascinated by myths and legends. Tiger Hill is like a ruin of classicism, preserving many ancient relics, but at the same time, it is like a garden of romanticism, with many strange and bizarre legends behind these ancient objects. Originally, classicism and romanticism have a related relationship, because a fascination with the old easily leads one away from real life and into fantasy. This fantasy that deviates from real life easily carries a romantic color. Observing everything in Suzhou with this hypothesis may not be entirely correct, but it is not far off.

(III) To the Lingering Garden in the Setting Sun

We came out of Tiger Hill and took a car to the Lingering Garden. Along the way, desolate grass covered many tombs, and the tombstones were as dense as bamboo shoots in spring. The setting sun slowly went down, illuminating the clouds into various colors, setting off the distant mountain scenery, causing us to look around from time to time. In the sound of wheels and horses' hooves, everything seemed to pass by like scenes in a movie. Finally, under a few green trees, we arrived at the Lingering Garden. After paying the fare and buying tickets, we began to tour the Lingering Garden. When we stepped into the Lingering Garden, the first impression that caught our eyes was the complete map of the Lingering Garden. It was completely built according to the Grand View Garden in "Dream of the Red Chamber," and it can also be said to be a miniature of the Grand View Garden. It completely represents the ideal buildings of our country hundreds of years ago. It is like a beauty in ancient costume, without any of the current Europeanized habits. Its architecture is very exquisite, with winding corridors and winding stone paths. Everything is completely man-made. When we went inside, the first thing we saw was weeping willows and ancient trees with branches, a long wooden bridge, with bridge railings on both sides, and clear green water under the bridge. There are also mountain roads stacked with artificial rocks, winding and twisting, so although the area is not large, it is quite attractive. Outside the artificial rock road, there are many winding corridors and pavilions. The corridors are all made of square bricks, not very wide or very high, but therefore there is a quiet atmosphere. There is no strong sunlight to oppress you, only faint light penetrates in.

My Sister's Love—Ms. Peng Xuezhen

—

I tell you, my sister has changed in the past six months. Look at her, she was always like a child, jumping and skipping like a bird on a branch. She had no worries or concerns, acting coquettishly in front of her mother and laughing innocently among her friends.

Growing up, she had naturally never thought about love. Nor had I ever imagined that my sister would be like any other grown-up girl, swept up in the waves of love.

It was in the depths of spring this year that my sister wrote to say: "Mom, I'm embarrassed to tell you, but Ke and I are getting engaged soon. We've known each other for a year, and our feelings are really good. Honestly, I never thought that the god of love would ever catch me. Lately, when I look in the mirror, I feel like I'm standing on the edge of youth, just like the depth of spring. But youth is fleeting and can never be recovered. Mom, don't make fun of me!"

I was stunned. I had never imagined that my sister would ever be immersed in a sea of love. I forgot that she was standing on the edge of youth. I forgot that Cupid's golden arrows are constantly being shot at young girls. In my mind, there was only the image of my sister's boldness and straightforwardness, but not a hint of a profile hiding in a lover's embrace, whispering secrets.

I smiled slightly.

During the summer vacation, worried about her mother, my sister reluctantly returned from the frontier in the scorching heat.

Ke in the photos was very handsome, kind of gentle, but couldn't shake off that particularly dignified air of Northerners.

"You two are really meant to be. I thought my sister would never be able to love anyone."

For the first time, I saw a particularly beautiful, shy blush spread across her cheeks.

To see my sister's embarrassed smile, all I had to say was something like, "Ke is thinking about you!" It was common for her to wait foolishly at the door for a letter, and when it arrived, she would turn it over and over for half an hour, reading it. When she was disappointed, she would pout and secretly scold the heartless postman. I really shouldn't have teased her so much that she didn't know whether to laugh or cry, and ended up chasing me around the yard to beat me.

In the evenings, while everyone was waving palm-leaf fans and enjoying the cool in the yard, my sister would always write letters to Ke alone upstairs.

"Go look at the stars! It's too hot under the lamp! Ha, what do you call him? Sweetie or darling..."

"You nosy ghost, it's none of your business!"

I would try to take a peek, and if she wouldn't let me, I would steal a glance at the scraps she had finished writing. She would scold me for being immoral, but I didn't care!

"I really can't figure out why, but I'm in a daze all day long. I'm afraid people will laugh at me, so I just pretend to be calm. As usual, my heart races when I read your letters. I'm really afraid of your sharp eyes, but I still have to read them again and again. I just hope the days fly by, and when the cool breeze blows away this heat, we can shake hands."

I don't know if the days actually flew by, but my sister finally left home eight or nine days earlier than planned, although everyone at the station couldn't help but have tears in their eyes.

In her letters, my sister often mentioned Ke, saying that he was a very loyal and lively child, and that she was happy.

A Full Length Novel

The Crossroads of the Era and Love (28)

— Zhang Ziping

Just when they were both away, the waiter brought the bill. Haiquan was embarrassed not to take it. He looked at it; it was only 2.46 yuan. Although he was a little reluctant, he felt the amount wasn't too much. He took his small wallet from his pocket, took out three silver dollars, and paid the waiter.

Cao Shiguang came back out from inside, smiling as he buttoned his pants. After sitting down, he poured himself tea and drank it without asking whether the bill had been paid. When he saw the waiter bringing the change, he pretended to be surprised.

"The bill's here? Let me pay… that won’t do… Lao Lin, sorry about that."

"It's nothing," Haiquan said, but he was still somewhat scornful of this religious man.

"Lao Cao!"

Mr. Liao staggered in from outside. He called out "Lao Cao!" then coughed for a while.

"Did you call him? What's the situation?"

"Cough cough! He's not home."

Haiquan looked at Mr. Liao's serious attitude, then at Cao Shiguang's smiling face. He suspected they had planned to trick him into treating them to this meal.

(XIII)

After leaving the restaurant, the three of them walked along the street on Wuma Road for a while. Cao Shiguang stayed close behind Liao Haifeng, whispering incessantly. He seemed to have forgotten that Haiquan was walking behind them. Seeing them having eaten their fill, wiping their greasy mouths, and ignoring him, Haiquan felt exceptionally indignant, and a feeling like being abandoned in the desert by his companions arose.

"Lao Cao!"

He called out to Cao Shiguang from behind. However, Cao Shiguang only turned his head to look at him, his face showing a doubtful expression, as if asking Haiquan why he was calling him.

"I'm going back."

"Isn't it nice to walk around?"

"I have schoolwork tomorrow."

Haiquan's voice was unhappy.

"I'm really sorry, we've really bothered Mr. Lin today."

Liao Haifeng said, stepping forward to cup his fist at Haiquan, his intention seemed to be hoping Haiquan would leave them quickly, because Haiquan's intuition was very sharp. He was genuinely angry with them, but he forced himself to endure it. He only nodded at them and turned to walk towards the bus stop. He only took three or four steps when he suddenly heard Cao Shiguang chasing after him, calling his name. He quickly stopped.

"Lao Lin, I'm really sorry about today…"

As he spoke, he hooked his arm over Haiquan’s shoulder, acting like one of the young hooligans on Fourth Horse Road.

“…you ended up spending a lot of money. We'll treat you another day."

"It's nothing."

Finance

The Silver Market During the Bank Holiday

Silver Exchange Rate Softens, Silver Discount is a Bank Loan

Single-Cent Coins Surge in the Morning, Rebound at Noon

Copper Coins Remain Unchanged, Double-Cent Coins as Before

Yesterday, due to the bank holiday, business was as calm as usual. The trading volume of silver in the market was also very low. Prices mostly softened. The morning market was 7 qian 1 fen 4 li 6 hao 2 hu and a half. The afternoon market was 7 qian 1 fen 4 li, resulting in a slight drop of half a li. The silver discount for both morning and afternoon markets was a bank loan, making the situation even weaker. Outward remittances were 570,000 in the morning market and 645,000 in the afternoon market. Banknotes were 45,000 in the morning market and 20,000 in the afternoon market. Off-market banknotes were 85,000 in the morning market and 30,000 in the afternoon market. Checks were 45,000 in the morning market and 10,000 in the afternoon market. In bank transactions, (Chinese merchants) mutual market was 500,000 in the morning market and 550,000 in the afternoon market. Receipts and payments between various bank silver accounts were over 400,000. Receipts and payments of money shop silver public notes were over 7.3 million. Receipts and payments of silver public notes were over 2.7 million. Receipts and payments of silver remittances were over 900,000. Receipts and payments of silver transfer accounts were over 2 million. Various receipts and payments of Chinese banks were around 3 million, with settlements over 2 million. Huai warehouse was 300,000. Small money shop transactions were over 300,000. In subsidiary coins, the price of Jiangsu small silver coins suddenly surged to 6 qian 5 fen in the morning market for no reason, with a transaction volume of 22,000 jiao. The price fell back again in the afternoon market, remaining at 6 qian 3 fen 8 li, with a transaction volume of 4,000 jiao. The morning market price of Guangdong small silver coins was 6 qian 2 fen and a half li, and the afternoon market price was 6 qian 2 fen. The transaction volume was 75,000 jiao in the morning market and 20,000 jiao in the afternoon market. The price of copper coins remained at 393,500 wen per thousand, with a transaction volume of over 38,500 strings of wen.

Public Bond Futures Rebound by 7-8 Jiao

February Futures Have Opened in Several Varieties

Trading Suspended Today Due to Futures Settlement

Yesterday (the 27th), the market conditions for various bonds on the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange were still scarce, with only 14,000 yuan changing hands for futures on the entire day. February futures have officially begun trading. For example, unified salt tax, 20-year bonds, demobilization, and troop reduction bonds have all been opened, but unified tax and salt tax bonds were traded more actively. The January futures market was still good, and buying and selling were not deserted. As for the trend of various bonds, prices had fallen sharply in recent days. Furthermore, the diplomatic situation with Japan was not as serious as previously rumored. Financial institutions in the local area were still mostly engaged in acquisitions. As a result, market sentiment slightly stabilized. Apart from sluggish opening prices in the early morning, prices then fluctuated and strengthened. The afternoon opening was the strongest, but the closing price turned loose again. As a result, the prices rebounded by about 7-8 jiao compared to the previous day. However, spot prices for salt tax, 20-year customs bonds, long-term financial bonds, and small 19-year customs bonds had no trading in recent days, so their prices fell quite sharply compared to before. The bond market's situation appeared chaotic again. Also, the market was suspended today due to settlement.
