Cotton Yarn

Yarn Market Shows Slight Improvement

｜Relying on the Strength of the Cotton Market｜

The cotton yarn market shows a slight recovery, with raw cotton prices remaining firm, causing some speculators to be bullish. However, in reality, there are still no good signs. Looking back at the domestic situation, it is extremely urgent. Moreover, the world's commerce is in a slump. How can the market have a large rise? Therefore, some manufacturers still hold the doctrine of buying when prices rise, but at present, with the help of the cotton market, there may be a small temporary increase in hope.

Near-Month Yarn Slightly Better by 3-4 Qian

Opening on the Renbiao front market, following the momentum of the cotton market from the previous day, it rose by 2, 4, and 5 qian. With the second and third markets lacking buyers, the market fell again. As a result, each month rose by 2, 3, and 4 qian. In the afternoon, hearing that actual demand was sluggish, the market atmosphere was again tired. However, the general intention of speculation and absorption was very strong. Each month fell by 2 qian. The total transaction volume for the day was 24,400 bales. It was found that Changfeng sold 3,100 bales, Gengfeng 1,000 bales, Shenji 650 bales, and Yiyu 500 bales. Cotton Market Surges in the Morning, Falls in the Afternoon

｜Ultimately, There is Not Much Change｜

Cotton prices rose sharply in the morning and fell in the afternoon. The short squeeze of this month's cotton was the most severe, but the result was still a peaceful situation. In fact, the overall situation is calm, yarn sales are sluggish, and factories are less interested in receiving high-priced cotton. However, some speculators, seeing that factories have not purchased foreign cotton this year, believe that there is a cotton shortage, and are wholeheartedly inclined to buy and go long. The market situation is tight. As for foreign cotton, it is currently difficult to calculate due to the impact of exchange rates. However, the difference is still about two taels (the spot price of American cotton middling is 29 taels and 1 qian in the American silver market), plus 7 taels for shipping to Shanghai. This is the raw material that can be spun into 32-count yarn.

Grain

Out-of-Province Rice Sales Boom, Spurring a Rise of Half a Yuan

Yesterday, there were not many out-of-province indica rice arrivals, and even fewer out-of-province Yuan rice arrivals. However, the Min Province merchants were actively purchasing, and their appetite was extremely strong. Although hoarding households stopped, market prices rose instead. There is not much out-of-province Yuan rice stored in Shanghai, and the quality is better than Du Yuan rice. Furthermore, it can be directly transshipped. Therefore, the Quanzhou and Fuzhou merchants from Min Province continued to purchase actively. However, the Shanghai inventory had already been purchased by the Min merchants, and there were not many new arrivals. Yesterday, a small number of Wuhu Yuan rice arrived and was completely purchased by the Min merchants. The inventory was also being scoured. A total of 901 bales of Wuhu machine-milled Yuan rice were opened, with prices jumping from 10 yuan to 10 yuan 3 jiao and a half, then further to 10 yuan 5 jiao, a large increase of half a yuan compared to the opening price of the previous day. The prices of indica rice from Jiangxi and Hunan were also driven up by several fen to nearly a jiao. It is recorded that 580 bales of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice were opened, with prices ranging from 8 yuan 5 jiao to 8 yuan 4 jiao and a half. 620 bales of Hunan machine-milled oil rice were opened, with prices ranging from 8 yuan 9 jiao to 8 yuan 6 jiao 7 fen. 260 bales of Hunan machine-milled Jing rice were opened, with prices ranging from 8 yuan 4 jiao and a half to 8 yuan 1 jiao and a half, all purchased by the Quanzhou and Fuzhou merchants from Min Province.

Flour Market Rises in the Afternoon

｜Short Covering... Very Good Actual Sales｜

Yesterday, the flour market was generally calm after opening in the morning, with no reports from the foreign wheat market. However, industry insiders believed that the supply of current flour was not abundant, so they remained firm on keeping prices high. Huafeng slightly reduced its offer, and the market seemed stable. Due to a lack of selling from various factories in the forward market and strong buying interest, market sentiment was quite good. In the afternoon, the market became even more active. Short covering was necessary for the current month due to only half-day trading, leading to gradual price increases. The forward market also saw step-by-step increases due to strong interest from actual sales customers. Regarding the current flour situation, Fuxin had already sold out, and Hezhong had no stock. Fufeng, Shenren, Xinda, and Huafeng all directly charged standard prices without adding extra. Whether prices can be stabilized will depend on the smooth import of foreign wheat. In the end, the current month was up by 0.02 yuan from the previous day, January up by 0.015 yuan, February up by 0.01 yuan, March up by 0.0175 yuan, April up by 0.01 yuan, and May up by 0.0075 yuan.

Rice Market Situation Stabilized

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, there were about 30 suppliers, and the stocks in the wharves were not abundant. City and rural stores were sluggish, mainly due to tight monetary conditions. All anticipated looser conditions. Superior japonica rice prices continued to fall by 0.01 yuan. Early and late rice arrivals were also connected. Sales in this area remained weak, with some interest from Tianjin. Market prices were slightly adjusted. Superior Dujian rice was in short supply, and prices rose by 0.015 yuan. Yinhua rice arrivals were moderate, and retail sales were not weak. Liquor sellers were active but hesitant. Market prices remained unchanged. Bianyuan rice was scarce, resulting in a lack of market activity.

(Xinzha) Yesterday, there were about 36-37 suppliers, but the outbound flow remained sluggish. River accumulations were still heavy. Limited high-quality northern japonica rice was offered, and bulk prices fell by about 0.01-0.02 yuan. Early and late rice arrivals and sales were both weak. The Bianyuan rice market lacked activity. The trend of Dujian rice from other ports showed signs of improvement. Daily sales totaled around 3,000 shi.

Wheat Market Temporarily Shows Signs of Easing

Yesterday, the wheat market generally remained stable. Due to the halt in foreign wheat trading, transactions were few. Furthermore, current auctions are for far-term deliveries. Given the scarcity of domestic wheat, future deliveries will likely be difficult. The only hope lies in foreign wheat. However, various factories are unable to deliver due to tight flour supplies. The tightness in January is mainly due to this. However, a ship of foreign wheat recently arrived and berthed at buoy number 7. It is said to be destined for several small and medium-sized factories, about 8 or 9 in total (excluding Xin and Fufeng). Unloading has been ongoing since yesterday. If more shipments arrive subsequently, the wheat market may temporarily ease. In the end, January was up by 0.012 yuan, March remained unchanged, and there was no comparison for April and May.

Vegetable Oil is in Short Supply, Prices Rise

Yesterday, the oilseed and miscellaneous grains market saw further improvements compared to the previous day. Outbound flows for various suppliers remained strong. Small soybeans were actively purchased by local factories, and prices increased by a few cents. Doudou soybeans from Guangdong also saw good outbound flow, and prices rose by 0.05-0.06 yuan, leading to increased activity in the soybean market. Transactions included 220 bags of Pudong Doudou soybeans, 300 bags of Pinghu Doudou soybeans, and 100 bags of Chongming Shayellow soybeans, all purchased by Guangdong suppliers. Additionally, 278 bags of Jiangbei yellow soybeans, three cartloads of Zhengyangguan yellow soybeans, and 1,200 bags of Andong Shayellow soybeans were purchased by local factories. Outbound flow for various sesame seeds was also good. 170 bags of Linhuaiguan flower sesame seeds were sold to foreign firms. Eight bags of Jiujiang milk sesame seeds and twelve bags of snow sesame seeds were purchased by Fuzhou suppliers. The peanut market showed some improvement with good outbound flow. 400 bags of Qinhuangdao peanuts and 45 bags of Tancheng peanuts were sold, all to Guangdong suppliers. The oil market saw a sharp rise in vegetable oil prices. Soybean oil prices remained stable. Vegetable oil prices rose due to shortages and strong outbound flow. Initially, prices remained flat, but they soon soared by 0.04-0.05 yuan. The main reason for this was the lack of available stock. The destinations were mainly local merchants and suppliers from Quanzhou and Xinghua.

Sugar Market

Fresh Chaoqing Sugar Arrives Today

Totaling 2,200 Bags

Medium Granulated White Sugar Opens at 14.8 Taels

Yesterday, the sugar market trend remained stable. The association's auction of common grade coarse granulated white sugar opened at 15.85 taels, but suppliers from Huai only offered 15.825 taels. The two sides held firm, and no deal was made. Several hundred bags of No. 8 Dutch Red sugar were auctioned at 11.7 taels, later rising to 11.75 taels, an increase of 0.05 yuan from the previous day. No. 18 Medium Granulated White, Huaxin goods, had been consistently maintained for days. Yesterday, they achieved their goal, opening with 1,000 bags at 14.8 taels. The remaining balance of Fresh Chaoqing sugar was 300 bags. Yesterday, they were fully sold. High Grade Blue opened at 9.05 taels, High Half South Blue at 8.7 taels, followed by 8.6-8.55 taels. According to a telegram from Shantou, the Yisheng ship had already departed from the area, carrying a total of 2,200 bags and expected to arrive this morning.

North-South Goods

Quanzhou Dried Longan Supply Greatly Reduced

The remaining stock of previous batches of Quanzhou dried longan is nearing depletion. Since costs must be covered, subsequent batches will be scarce. According to a telegram yesterday, only slightly over 700 boxes were shipped and should arrive in Shanghai soon.

Silk and Tea

Old Factory Silk Sales Are Not Weak

Sales of white factory silk to Europe and America have declined sharply. Old silk stocks are abundant, and silk prices have plummeted. Recently, inland silk factories have been using new-style silks for both domestic and international sales. Seeing that old factory silk prices have fallen to the lowest levels and native silk is of poor quality and labor-intensive, they are switching to factory silk to weave high-quality linings, spring hair fabrics, etc. The overall cost is still considered worthwhile. Therefore, since the beginning of autumn, inland silk factories have purchased a total of 1,753 bales of old factory silk in Shanghai. Besides being shipped back to their respective factories, 296 bales of old factory silk purchased by various silk factories remain in Shanghai warehouses.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Tanyan

Reply to Mr. Li Weinian's Letter

— Buddha

Your letter states that recently, the respect for teachers has declined, and the academic atmosphere is turbulent, which is a hidden concern for the future of education. Recently, I read two articles in your publication, "Tomorrow's Paper is Due" and "Small Hall Name." The content of these articles not only insults teachers but also greatly damages students' character. Such records are not something your publication should include.

"The decline of respect for teachers and the turbulence of the academic atmosphere" is indeed as you said, worthy of a great sigh. However, my opinion differs slightly from yours. You believe that such writings should not be published to prevent further decline and turbulence. Your intention is to hide the flaws and prevent them from being exposed, which is indeed a motherly heart. However, this publication publishes such writings to encourage people to correct their mistakes if they have them, and to be more cautious if they don't. It is intended to promote good and punish evil. Therefore, although our goals are the same, our views differ.

"The decline of respect for teachers and the turbulence of the academic atmosphere" did not start today. Assuming that this publication does not publish such writings, the respect for teachers will not decline, and the students will not be turbulent. Now, publishing these writings does indeed have the risk of tempting students to fall and commit crimes, which is something we should not do. If such writings are not published, and the respect for teachers has already declined, and the students have already become turbulent, then the reasons for their decline and turbulence are very complex, and I will not elaborate on them here. In short, this publication will never dare to take responsibility for it.

However, because of this, I want to study the general psychological state of students. Is it inherently good or inherently evil? When this publication records such writings, do students consider it a disgrace and a loss of student character and improve, or do they consider it novel and pleasing, and consider it worthy of emulation? Assuming that students consider it a great disgrace and a loss of student character, and there is nothing that can be done to improve them, then I have nothing more to say. If students consider it a great disgrace and a loss of student character and warn each other not to commit such acts in the future, then what this publication has published may not be an intention to promote good and punish evil. Although I dare not claim credit for it, I can indeed disclaim responsibility. Furthermore, since its reform, this publication has not only been like this towards the academic community but also towards all the dark secrets of society. It has spared no effort to expose them and describe them, fighting to the death with the dark secrets. This is also its stance. It will never promote them further just because their secrets are not dark enough, adding another layer of color to them. Hiding evil and promoting good is originally the attitude of sages. Not washing dirty linen in public is originally a bad habit under the patriarchal system. Now, we want to use another method to break through all the dark secrets and all the bad habits, leaving them with no foothold. We are unwilling to continue condoning evil and covering up mistakes, specializing in putting on a show, while the inside is still dark and the outside is still civilized. This is the pain that China has suffered for thousands of years and the cause of corruption accumulated over thousands of years. My humble opinion is such. I wonder what you think of it, sir?

A Farmer's Words

— Guangxin

With several friends, taking advantage of the warm sun, I went for a walk in the suburbs. Accidentally, I came to the front of a village with thatched and tile houses. I saw a farmer in his forties, alone beside a field of green and yellow vegetables, talking to himself like a madman. We were very curious, so we approached him and began to ask him questions.

"This year's grain harvest is very good. This year, bandits have not patronized this place either. This is probably because the heavens have pity on you. You can have a comfortable year this year!"

"Sir, how do you know our suffering? We can't even think about a moment of peace or a full meal, let alone a comfortable year!"

As he spoke, his "brows were furrowed," showing a pitiful appearance, and he sighed a long sigh!

We asked him in surprise, "What is the reason for this?"

"Sir, the bandits in the past few years have made this place a mess, unable to cultivate. Last year's floods washed away all the houses. These years of misfortune have left me with a debt-ridden body. The interest rate is four or five percent, and the interest is calculated on top of the interest. In less than three years, it has already exceeded one and a half times the principal. This year's grain harvest is relatively good, but the price of grain is really cheap. The people who are demanding payment come to the door to urge me every day, forcing me to have no choice but to carry the grain to the nearby market town to sell it. The general business owners ignore you. After you ask annoyingly, they turn around and say very pretentiously, 'How much money do you want?' Poor me, I am also very hungry, my spirit is also tired, and I have no energy to speak. At this time, I have to answer respectfully... 'Listen to you, sir!' Then he will say very vigorously... 'Yesterday, the market price of grain was two yuan, three jiao, and five fen per shi. Today, it will fall by two jiao and five fen. Are you willing?' At this time, I am in a dilemma and have to sell the grain. One shi of grain sold for two yuan and one jiao of foreign money, and it takes a day's work. It turns out that it only sells for more than one yuan. At this price, it is not even enough for half of the cost of cultivation. Even if all of this year's grain is sold, it is not enough for this year's interest! And my family has seven mouths to feed. Where can we have a full meal? The bandits of the past few years and the floods of last year have forced us to flee to the famine far away. Therefore, the land taxes of the past few years have not been paid off. Unexpectedly, during this year's autumn harvest, the county sent more than a dozen soldiers as fierce as wolves to the countryside. Their mission is... 'To collect all the arrears and pre-collect the new grain.' As a result, my soul was lost in fright, and I couldn't speak for half a day. Those fierce-looking soldiers said very viciously... 'You hurry up and get money to pay for our travel expenses. Each of us wants eight jiao of foreign money per day. If you wait until tomorrow, you will have to pay even more. Hurry up and get it...'

Poor me, I was forced to cry at the time, and I couldn't say a word.

They said even more viciously... 'The officials are not afraid of your poverty, and the ghosts are not afraid of your thinness.' What's the use of crying? We just want money anyway.

At this time, I had no choice but to go to the neighbors on the left and right to borrow money. I didn't know that they were in the same boat as me and had to prepare money to pay for the soldiers' expenses. Their men had all gone out to get money, and several women were in a panic at home. I had no choice but to come back. They | the soldiers, then roared... 'Where is the money!' At this time, I said in a trembling voice, 'No...' Before I could finish speaking, I was hit on the head several times. At this time, my wife and children saw this situation and cried loudly. I couldn't help but cry loudly too! In the end, I had to sell my fifty-yuan plow cattle for twenty-seven yuan of foreign money in pain, and used more than ten yuan to pay for the expenses of the soldiers | the soldiers, and even killed a breeding chicken for them to eat before they left. When they left, they said with strange eyes, 'You have to pay off everything within three days, otherwise we will come again!'

Sir, our grain and rations, accumulated over the years, require more than thirty yuan of foreign money to be paid off. Where can I get it within three days?

At this time, if I die! Then the whole family will perish together! If I live! I'm afraid I won't live long!

When he said this, he couldn't help but shed tears again.

In our hearts, we couldn't help but shed tears of sympathy.

"The rural economy is bankrupt," "Farmers are crying bitterly," How would we know their suffering? As for those important people who live in foreign-style houses, it goes without saying.

We also have a considerable understanding of the saying that "Oppressive government is fiercer than a tiger."

This farmer's words, I came from my hometown | Hunan, the real situation, but yesterday I went to Wuxi with a friend, this kind of "economic bankruptcy" situation is almost the same as ours | Hunan, with emotion, I drafted this article.

A Jin

— Wenbing

A Jin was originally a farmer's daughter, growing up in the countryside. She had her own peaceful world, and she also had her own imaginative life.

In the spring, early in the morning, she would lead a strong water buffalo, stepping on the bright, dewy grass, to the hillsides and open fields to graze. She had no feelings for the beauty of nature. She just led the cattle to eat grass. Others sang folk songs, but she didn't sing, and she even pretended not to listen. She really looked like a country girl.

Summer came, and she had to do other farm work. Although her feet were bound, her legs were still strong. In June, she did water-pumping work, and she was almost as good as a young man in his twenties.

Autumn was also very busy. When harvesting rice, she had to take on part of the rice-cutting work. After that, all the rice straw from dozens of acres of fields

Page 18

was collected by her two hands and piled up in the empty space in the back garden.

Only in winter did she have relatively more free time. In fact, not really. Every day, in addition to helping her sister-in-law cook and make tea, she would shut herself in her room all day long spinning yarn and weaving hemp. Because she was not young anymore—she was already sixteen years old. On the third day of the third month, she had been betrothed to Liu Axi, whom she often thought about. Precisely because of this, she not only felt that she was gradually changing physically, but her mind was also obviously different. The most obvious thing was that she had her period every month… When she had nothing to do, she would always sit there blankly in a daze. Usually, Xiangda next door would flirt with her and even touch her hand, but she didn't feel anything… But now, she no longer tolerated such actions from Xiangda. She thought it was an act of insulting women. If a woman tolerated such an insult, then that woman was simply not a woman. However, she was full of yearning in her mind for what a fun life it would be!

She kept secretly inquiring about the news of her marriage, but it often disappointed her, and Axi had gone to the city to work instead. She heard that it would take a long time before he could bring her over to get married. She thought… "Why be so slow?"

From then on, she fantasized more and more about the scenery in the city. Xiangda had also told her that Li Siye from Ao had been to the city once and said that he didn't need to cook. When he was hungry, he could run to a restaurant to eat… He didn't need to rent a house. He could spend the night in a hotel… It was especially convenient to go out. He could take a rickshaw, a tram, and even a fast-moving car… There were also… what kind of cars to take… When it came to playing, there were endless good things to say. There were shadow puppet shows to watch, live tigers to see, and the Great World had giant tortoises that were thousands of years old to see. Sometimes, there were conjoined twins preserved in medicine on the side of the road to see. There were also people who were taller than a zhang, and there were also people who were only two chi tall. In short, the good things in the city were ten thousand times better than in the countryside, A Jin thought.

But she also had doubts and dissatisfaction. That was that there were groups of women who would go out to find men to play with in the evening… Those women were simply not women. It was rare to find them in the countryside. Therefore, she didn't quite believe Xiangda's words about this, thinking that Xiangda was deliberately lying.

However, the city should be good overall. Axi went to the city to work. Wasn't he happy and fortunate?

Axi's cousin, Guisheng, was originally her buffalo-herding friend. Because she and Axi were engaged, Guisheng often came to her house to play. Her parents didn't guard against him, because he was the younger brother of her future son-in-law. Sometimes, she would talk and laugh with him generously and casually. Once, Guisheng said to her… "Big brother is having a lot of fun in the city. I want you to go to the city to play too!" When she heard this, she was shy at first, and didn't commit one way or the other. Later, she thought to herself… "Wouldn't that be good? If he takes me there… Anyway, I really want to see Axi's face!"

So A Jin eloped to the city with Guisheng.

Just that Guisheng was smart, he took her to a different city.

Leather Coats and Donations

— Xuyu

The weather was cold. Miss Wang opened a box and looked at the box full of winter clothes. She said coquettishly to Old Master Wang… "Dad, I don't like the leather coat I made last year anymore. Give me two hundred yuan so I can make a new one."

"What? You want to make another coat? Do you know how many you already have? How much money did you spend in total?"

"How could I not know? I only have eight leather coats in total. Each one costs an average of one hundred and sixty yuan, which only costs more than one thousand and two hundred yuan. What's so rare about that?"

"Humph, you've already spent more than one thousand yuan on coats alone. Isn't that rare? Besides, the leather of your coat is very good, and the foreign wool lining, which costs more than three yuan a foot, is also the best you picked. How can you just put it aside after wearing it for only one winter? This bad habit of liking the new and disliking the old is not only undesirable, but such waste of resources is even more sinful…"

Old Master Wang was giving a long lecture, saying a few words of righteous instruction. Unfortunately, Mrs. Wang in the inner room heard it and defended her daughter… "What do you mean by wasting resources? A daughter like her, born into a family like ours, don't say just one coat that costs two hundred yuan that has been worn for a winter, even if she wears several in a winter, it's not a big deal. You can't bring money into the world when you're born, and you can't take it with you when you die. How can you, such a wealthy father, be so stingy?"

Old Master Wang couldn't argue with his wife and daughter, so he had to sign a check for two hundred yuan in pain and went out to the office reluctantly.

Before the gate was closed, three patriotic youths walked into the house, holding bamboo donation tubes and donation registers. They bowed to Mrs. Wang and said… "The weather is cold, and the borders are bitterly cold. The birds and beasts have hidden away. It is pitiful that our volunteer soldiers who are fighting the enemy for the country are still wearing their lined clothes and fighting hard in the icy and snowy fields. There is an urgent need for winter clothes. Please, madam, be generous and donate some money."

Mrs. Wang retracted her loving smile towards her daughter and replied coldly… "Since the volunteer soldiers lack winter clothes, who told them to risk their lives with the Japanese in the cold and windy northeast? Even if they freeze to death, what does it have to do with me? At this time of the year, when the economy is difficult, we are worried about freezing and starving even after economizing on food and clothing. Who has the spare money to donate to them?"

Mrs. Wang's attitude of rejecting people from a distance actually "didn't cost a penny" and issued an "order to leave" as if to chase the three patriotic youths out.

Shop Clerk Correspondence

Marriage Problems That Cause Sleeplessness and Loss of Appetite

Editor Sir,

I am originally a child from a village forty or fifty li away from Shanghai. My family is very poor. My father is a peddler in Shanghai—selling vegetables. My mother plants five mu of rented land in the countryside. The family's expenses all depend on my father's hard support. Living in such a difficult environment, I naturally did not have the opportunity to receive a proper education. So I helped my mother farm and make a living. But how can I maintain it for a long time on these few mu of rented land? Moreover, agriculture has been on the verge of bankruptcy in recent years. Later, through the introduction of my father's friend, I worked as a worker in a printing factory in Zhabei. During the unprecedented disaster of the "January 28th Incident," that printing factory was also sacrificed in the artillery fire of Japanese imperialism. Therefore, I lost my job as a result!

This summer, after thinking of all kinds of ways, I finally got introduced by a relative to be an apprentice in a store, and the bread problem was temporarily solved.

Recently, my family suddenly started to make a fuss about my marriage. I was betrothed to a girl from the same village by my parents when I was young. My mother's letter said… "…I am already fifty years old. I am old and weak, and I am about to die. I want to marry you off and finish this wish of mine. I think at the latest when you are nineteen years old, I will definitely marry you. Moreover, there are few people in the family, so it would be good to marry one back earlier to help me with my work. In case I get sick, there will be someone to take care of me. What do you think?"

When I received this letter, I really couldn't make up my mind. Although I am only seventeen years old and have two years to consider, should I agree to do this? Or how should I refuse? I have three difficulties…

㈠ The usual apprenticeship period is three years. I will not be a fully qualified master in two years, and my personal finances will not be sufficient. How can I afford it…

㈡ If I write back to refuse, then my elderly parents will definitely be sad. If they get sick from worry, how can I face them…

㈢ How can I rashly marry a woman I have never met? If I get married, can we grow old together?

This problem has been lingering in my mind for dozens of days. Just when I was wandering and restless, I suddenly saw the "Shop Clerk Correspondence" column in your newspaper, which is dedicated to solving difficult problems for us. Therefore, I also want to trouble you to give me a perfect gospel.

Sincerely, Xu Zhan

Editor's note: Xu Jun, at the age of seventeen, can be so aware of the hardships of life and is afraid of making his parents sad, so he does not dare to answer rashly. We don't need to put out the signboards of moralists such as "the decline of social morals" and "filial piety is commendable." We also want to express our infinite admiration for Xu Jun.

Now, there are countless people in Xu Jun's situation… I believe that there are also many who feel the same difficulties as Xu Jun. Therefore, we will make it public and attach our humble opinions for everyone's reference.

First, if you cannot afford it financially, it is of course better not to marry. But now, when women's employment is gradually expanding, women can generally make a living on their own and do not have to rely on men. Those with higher knowledge can be teachers or staff in various companies and institutions… Those with lower knowledge can also work in factories… or do sewing work on the streets… or wash clothes for others… They can use their abilities anytime and anywhere to exchange for the cost of living. However, you must understand the times and know that a life earned by hard work is sacred, and you must never think that it is "embarrassing."

At the same time, you must work hard in your job and never be pessimistic. You can naturally gain a position slowly. Read more books and newspapers in your spare time, and you can improve your knowledge. In the future, when you have a suitable opportunity, you may be able to engage in a better career.

Second, in the letter to your parents, you may as well gently state your difficulties and ask your parents to inquire whether the other party | your fiancée | has the ability to make a living. It would be even better if she does. If not, it is still possible to learn now. The timing can always be discussed. We think that you can temporarily not refuse, so that your parents can get some comfort.

Third, now, except for the intellectual class, most people still have old-fashioned marriages. Facts tell us that the results of absolute "freedom" are not necessarily perfect. This is probably because the parties involved are too enthusiastic when things happen and their judgment is too weak. We might as well change it a little now. Since it was your parents who betrothed you when you were young, you may as well take an opportunity to meet and talk with her, or continue to correspond, to see if she can be your lifelong partner. If there is no opportunity, then you can entrust your close friends in the countryside to visit her and ask about her character, whether she is gentle and kind, and whether she can endure hardship. If she is a very good woman, it is possible to "grow old together." And it can save a lot of trouble. If, after the investigation or meeting, you find that you are not satisfied, then you should resolutely make up your mind, tell your parents the pros and cons in front of them, and discuss the proper way to handle things. We know that parents always love their children. As long as they can help their son succeed, there is nothing they will not try to accommodate.

In short, parents marrying a daughter-in-law for their son is for the son and not for the parents themselves. Therefore, if the son firmly opposes it, the parents should give it the greatest consideration. That is the right thing to do.

Shop Clerk Correspondence Column Regulations

(1) Purpose of the Correspondence: The purpose of this column is to gather ideas, explain difficult problems, learn from each other, and improve the happiness of life.

(2) Target Audience: The target audience of this column is limited to shop clerks and apprentices in terms of people, and limited to this port in terms of location.

(3) Content of the Correspondence: All questions concerning personal daily life, such as…

(1) Occupation (2) Moral and academic cultivation (3) Entertainment and sports (4) Marriage, as well as other questions concerning the country and society, are all welcome. If the content of the questions is too profound and beyond the ability of this column, it can also be introduced to the "Reader Advisory" of this newspaper for answering.

(4) Method of Submission

(1) The letter must state the name, age, place of origin, occupation, and detailed mailing address, etc. It must still be stated when writing subsequent letters.

(2) The style of the letter is not limited, but it should be simple and easy to understand, and it must be written clearly.

(3) Please write "Shenbao Newspaper, Port Zengkan, Shop Clerk Correspondence Column Received" on the letter. If you need a reply, please attach two fen of postage stamps.

(4) The sender must cut out the special stamp published by this column and paste it on the upper left corner of the letter. If it is not pasted, we will not reply.

(5) Handling Method After Receiving the Letter

(1) All questions discussed that this newspaper believes are of value to the public may be disclosed in the newspaper.

(2) In order to respect the opinions of the sender, if the letter states that they do not want their name to be disclosed, or that they need a separate reply, it can also be done.

(3) If the sender hopes that the letter will be disclosed in the newspaper, but it is too long and cannot be disclosed in full, it will be published concisely. Also, if the content of the question is complicated and has to be carefully studied, resulting in a late reply or disclosure, please forgive us.

(4) When there are many letters, we will answer them in the order in which they are received. If there is a delay, please forgive us.

Novels

Sympathizers (Continuation 7)

— Zhang Henshui

(4) Both Sides Sympathize

After a few sentences of conversation, Meng Guobao already knew that starting with principles was futile. Wang Laoer certainly didn't understand them. Even if he explained them in a refined and simple manner, he still wouldn't get it. To understand their suffering, one couldn't use objective methods to probe. It was better to ask him directly and let him speak for himself. These words shouldn't be followed by immediate explanations; one should wait and speak slowly later. Seeing Meng Guobao silent and not saying anything, Wang Laoer twisted the mouthpiece of his dry tobacco pipe in his palm for a moment. From a betel nut pouch hanging on his waistband, he took out a pinch of yellow tobacco shreds, pressed them onto the pipe bowl, then held the pipe stem with both hands, presenting it to Meng Guobao with a smile, "Have a smoke?" Meng Guobao said, "I don't do that." Wang Laoer smiled, "You're truly a wealthy man." He then put the pipe mouthpiece into his own mouth and puffed away, making "pu-ji, pu-ji" sounds. Then he shouted, "Bring a fire! Has the tea been brewed yet? The guest has been here for so long!" He raised his voice a little, facing inward, of course. This was speaking to the one who was tending the stove because that's how it was in Chinese families: when the man spoke loudly, it was to call his wife and daughters; when the woman spoke loudly, it was to call her husband. This was a foolproof method. The Second Sister-in-law came out in response to this shout. She carried two duck-egg-colored rough porcelain bowls in one hand and a tall-handled tile teapot in the other. As she stepped out of the doorway, she saw Meng Guobao squinting at her and called out, "Mr. Meng." She then retreated two steps. Wang Laoer put down his pipe, took the teapot and bowls, and poured tea into them. Because there was only one bench by the low table, he retreated backward, leaning against a stone mill frame, holding the rough porcelain bowl in both hands like a monkey holding a peach, with his mouth pointed towards the rim. Meng Guobao watched him pour a bowl of tea and place it on the edge of the table in front of him. Judging by the color, the tea was as yellow as horse urine, with many tea leaves forming a layer at the bottom of the bowl. The tea was steaming hot, with tea vapor rising into the air. Sniffing the vapor, it had the scent of green grass. Seeing Wang Laoer drink it with such relish, he also took a sip. It was both astringent and bitter, and seemed to have a salty taste. He immediately put the teacup down. Wang Laoer saw this and asked with a smile, "You're not used to this kind of tea, are you?" Meng Guobao smiled and said, "What's there to be unaccustomed to? You're a person, and I'm a person. If you can drink it, then I can drink it too." Wang Laoer understood these words and said with a smile, "Mr. Meng is really good. Not at all pretentious." As he spoke, Second Sister-in-law Wang leaned against the door frame leading inside, with one foot raised and resting on the threshold. Although her head was lowered, her eyes kept falling on Meng Guobao. When Meng Guobao occasionally turned to look at her, she lowered her head even further. Meng Guobao initially paid no attention to her and said to Wang Laoer, "It's not that I'm not pretentious, it's that I've thought things through. We're all people, we should all wear the same clothes and eat the same food. That's the right thing to do. But things in this world can't be that way. And the people who do the least work are the ones who eat the best and wear the best. Take farmers, for example. Some enjoy the good life, and some suffer. You're planting other people's fields. You should know how your rent and the landlord's share are divided, right?"

(To be continued)

Film Supplement

Republic of China, Year 21, December 28th, Wednesday (No Extra Charge)

World News

From Japan to China

— Ai

On the world stage... undeniably, everyone recognizes film as a powerful tool for social education. However, culture is time-sensitive, and we can imagine that film will certainly be used as another weapon!

Our eastern neighbor has now implemented film diplomacy. The national slogans are: "Film politicization," "Film propaganda," and "Film militarization!"

From the September 18th Incident to the present, if we were to investigate the cinemas in Japan, probably more than half of the films are about the Northeast. What is said in these films is nothing more than the spirit of the Yamato soul, the bravery of the samurai, the corruption of China, the incompetence of the Chinese army, and the self-liberation of the people of the Northeast.

They know that they are immature in the world of film and have no status, so the government has issued very strict orders and provided considerable economic assistance to various companies. This has mobilized the entire nation to unite externally and promote the country. For example, several films sent to Geneva were provided free of charge, and they will be sent to various countries for free public screenings in the future. This small nation can see through the financial losses and seek international sympathy for Japan's invasion, blaming the Shanghai Incident entirely on China.

This grand alliance of the Japanese film industry not only cannot find an opponent in the Far East, but no film industry group in the world has such great momentum. It is truly an unprecedented event. According to a report from the Japanese Ministry of Education, companies that specialize in filming such films now account for nine-tenths of the total number of Japanese film companies. "Shin興", "Kansai", "National", "Fukuda", "Akazawa", "Tokyo Kawai", "Dainikatsu", "Yoshikawa", "Matsushita Kamata"... none of them are not among them, abandoning all other types of films and devoting themselves to the Sino-Japanese Incident. From September 18th to today, more than four thousand productions have been produced, and it is estimated that by September 18th, 1933, the total will reach the round number of eight thousand sets. The later generations of the Japanese nation will certainly eat the consequences of this crazy "war-making" movement. Many of the exterior scenes in these films are taken from the Shanghai war. The rest also use real scenes from the Northeast. As for the actors, in addition to the original roles of each company, almost everyone from the Emperor to the lower-ranking officers who invaded China has appeared on camera.

Looking back at our country, what about us? The films produced are still about love, still about modernity, seemingly unaware of being oppressed, and that we should loudly call for saving the country through film. Occasionally, one or two films are successively made difficult by the Central Film Inspection Committee and the Concession Film Inspection Committee. In fact, what we have filmed is not even one ten-thousandth as effective as Japan's counter-propaganda.

I hope that our government and people will wake up! Arise in time!

Film Reviews

Gilded Love

— Jie

In the minds of today's youth, there is nothing more attractive than two things: money and love. Then "Platinum Blonde," which premiered at the Cathay Theater yesterday, is a film title that caters to people's tastes.

Love gilded with gold, in other words... love based on money, everyone knows that it is bound to fail. This film exposes this very essence. There are also many places in this film that mock the trivialization, bribery, and debauchery of people in the news industry. It does not lie; in fact, there is no shortage of such bad actors in the press. It also provides an introduction, saying what kind of person is the ideal lover, husband, or wife in the eyes of the opposite sex, and the pain suffered by people who marry for money (especially men on the poor side).

The story is simply told, and everything can be included in two sentences: a poor reporter meets and marries a wealthy woman for an interview and becomes her live-in husband. Because of mental oppression, he divorces and willingly lives with another woman in a very poor family.

However, there are many branches added to the film, so the story is stretched out for a long time. It was originally an ordinary comedy, but everywhere... almost every inch of film... is full of small interest, constantly making people laugh. These interpolations are not annoying... completely humorous, but not tiring, but there are some places that are out of touch with reason because we cannot treat it as a slapstick comedy.

Among the stars, Jean Harlow, who plays the merchant's daughter, is the most outstanding. Nominally a supporting role, she is actually the protagonist. Her dignified and luxurious demeanor is generous but not vulgar, like a maiden in a boudoir who is deeply in need of a man. Robert Williams, a lively young man, reveals his personality with interesting small actions and words. How strange that the director demoted Loretta Young, who is very capable of performing, to play the other woman, and did not give her a chance to act alone, except for a long shot of the two writing together. However, using her as an important supporting role does add a lot of brilliance to this film. The remaining actors all have the ability to be humorous and amusing, coupled with wonderful music, which is dedicated to winning with noise... without any humor. It can be regarded as a unique style. The cooperation of light and photography makes the scenery very grand and beautiful.

Comparing the merits and demerits of the comprehensive aspects, the director can be regarded as superior, and meticulousness is his strength.

This is all I saw in the whole film.

In a Few Words

Should There Be a "Break"?

— Zongwen

"Should a ten-minute break be added halfway through a movie?" This question is often mentioned in front of my friends, and their answers are no more than the following three:

A. The break allows us to have the opportunity to savor the script and guess the outcome of the story, which is a very interesting thing. (Referring to not reading the synopsis).

B. A person's eyes must take a break after watching a movie for an hour! Otherwise, they may be harmed, which is a very hygienic thing.

C. A break on the screen is a necessary thing, but it must be at the appropriate time.

Readers, do you think these reasons are sufficient?

Two Platinum Dragons Mutually Exploit

— Xing

The "Platinum Dragon" film of the Southern Film Company is currently in production. Xue Juexian became famous with the play "Platinum Dragon", and the Nanyang Tobacco Company also produced a type of "Platinum Dragon Cigarettes". However, Shanghai people only know the cigarette name and do not know that it is also the name of a play. It is said that the Nanyang Company had a whimsical idea and intended to ask the Southern Company's film to insert the canned appearance of "Platinum Dragon Cigarettes". Negotiations are currently underway.

Si Lang Visits His Mother on the Silver Screen

— Ying

As an annual practice, old theaters close for at least seven or eight days, which is a pity for those who are addicted to opera. This year, Tianyi Company has filmed a sound film "Si Lang Visits His Mother", which is co-starred by the female lead Xue Yanqin and Tan Fuying. Sitting in the Palace, Stealing the Order, Crossing the Pass, Seeing the Mother, Crying in the Hall, and Being Allowed to Take Back the Order are performed for a total of six quarters of an hour, about eight thousand feet long.

Chinese stage plays have been brought to the silver screen. There is an American film "Dr. Mei's Tiger Assassination", which is an imported product. This "Si Lang Visits His Mother" is the first Chinese self-made film. The script promotes Chinese "filial piety," "credibility," and art.

This film was produced by Tianyi's newly established "Agency Filming Department", so it is not purely a Tianyi production, but has the nature of a commission. The total cost is 30,000 yuan, and Huang and Tan each received 6,000 yuan. The attached picture is as follows...

Jeanette MacDonald's Little History

MacDonald is currently the most popular silver star on the film scene. Her works are warmly welcomed everywhere. Her singing and beautiful face are so charming and glamorous. She is a newly discovered silver star in Hollywood. Since co-starring with Chevalier in "The Love Parade," she has become famous throughout Europe. Then she starred in "The Vagabond King," "Monte Carlo," and "The Merry Widow," and then she soared to the highest peak of the silver screen.

Her family history is also very ordinary. She is British and grew up in Philadelphia, USA. Her father was once an actor. She also has an older sister who is a singer on the Broadway stage. Because she was still young, she followed her father to school in Philadelphia. She was naturally intelligent and was praised by teachers. At the same time, she paid great attention to other subjects. At the age of eight, she participated in a grand local gala and performed singing and dancing, which was appreciated by general playwrights.

At the age of fifteen, she went with her father from Philadelphia to Broadway to visit her sister. Unintentionally, she was spotted by the discerning eye of the theater manager, who insisted that she stay in the theater as a singer. So she left school and embarked on the stage. After three years of hard work, she gained a place on the stage and many immortal reputations. At this time, movies were popular all over the United States, and the singers on Broadway joined the silver screen one after another. But she was willing to stick to the old and unwilling to innovate until sound films began in Hollywood, and the film industry went straight to Broadway to search for talents. Jeanette was also recruited by the great director Lubitsch. She first co-starred with Chevalier in "The Love Parade," followed by "The Vagabond King," "The Merry Widow," "One Hour With You," and "Love Me Tonight." Although she once joined Fox Company and filmed a "The Smiling Lieutenant," she soon rejoined Paramount. She is already a popular celebrity. Her fiancé is called (Bob Ritchie), who is a wealthy young man. It is said that they will be married soon.

A Bundle of Tianyi News

— Sheng

Since Tianyi Company filmed the entire "Si Lang Visits His Mother" Peking opera for the Gu Feng Film Company, due to the clear pronunciation and exquisite scenery, a film company in Guangdong contacted Tianyi, wanting to film a Cantonese sound film "Platinum Dragon". It is said that negotiations were successful the day before yesterday, and yesterday afternoon they started filming the "Garden Scolding" scene.

Tianyi's "Poetry on Banana Leaves" and "Two Girls in the Northeast" (i.e., Two Orphaned Girls in the War Zone), which have been filmed but not yet released, will soon be successively premiered at the New Light Theater. The plot, sound, scenery, lighting, etc. of these two films are all excellent. It is expected that when they are released, they will definitely cause a sensation.

Rare News from the Film Industry

Tom Mix's Horse

— Ziyin

Martial arts star Tom Mix. His best skill is riding a horse, so he rides his horse in every film. Therefore, Tom Mix's horse has also become very famous. Its name is Tony, which many people know.

But one point that careless viewers will be deceived by is that although Tom is still Tom, his horse has now been replaced by a new generation. Horses don't live as long as humans, so the person is still as strong, but the horse has declined. This king of horses, Tony, is now leisurely enjoying his remaining years in the pasture.

Its replacement is its son, who has inherited its mantle. It is a tall and majestic horse, completely like its father in its prime. Its name is called Tony Jr. Ordinary people only remember the name Tony, but they don't know that it has already had a replacement.

Speaking of old Tony's retirement from the film industry, half of it was because he was old and not as agile as in the past, and half of it was because he encountered an accident at the end. That was during the filming of "Hidden Gold," when old Tony was unfortunately injured in the buttocks. Tom decided to give this loyal companion, who had been with him for many years, a good rest.

It is not certain whether little Tony can fulfill his duties in the future. However, rumors have already risen, saying that little Tony is a bit "out of tune".

That is entirely due to a recent incident of falling off a horse. The thing is like this. When filming that day, the horses were side by side, so little Tony, Tom's new mount, accidentally stepped into a mud pit. Its strength was far less than its father's, so it rushed forward, knocking Tom down and hitting him on a nail pile, causing Tom to injure three ribs and several internal injuries.

This martial arts star has already undergone surgery by a doctor and will soon recover. He still trusts his little Tony, and he says that they will definitely be able to cooperate with each other. This accident was just the first time.

We hope this is also the last time.
